Japan proposes to unilaterally abolish the treaty if its proposal cannot be agreed to by other countries. Japan also intends to conduct the preliminary conference through bilateral negotiations, opposing a roundtable conference. (Japan Union News dispatch, 20th)

(Tokyo) Japan will notify its intention to abolish the Washington Treaty. Britain and the United States have misunderstood this, believing that Japan will immediately carry out military expansion and even increase its fleet. In order to dispel this misunderstanding, the Imperial Government intends to clarify Japan's policy before notifying the abolition, that is, the Imperial Government will strictly abide by its obligations during the two-year period of the treaty's continued validity, as stipulated in Article 23, and will not build ships or expand its military. (Havas dispatch, 19th)

(London) The Associated Press has learned that the outcome of the naval talks may be a five-power naval treaty based on a semi-total tonnage system. According to this plan, countries will be allocated total tonnage for medium and light ships, such as cruisers, destroyers, and submarines, while the allocation of special tonnage will be limited to battleships, heavy cruisers, and aircraft carriers. The signatory countries can freely build cruisers, destroyers, and submarines within the tonnage limit. According to reliable sources, Japan wants to propose a complete tonnage system. In view of Britain's opposition, Japan is using a semi-tonnage system as a compromise solution. It is heard that Britain may support this proposal. International Air Race Began at 6:30 AM Yesterday 35

An Unprecedented Feat in Aviation History

From London to New Gold Mountain, a Distance of Ten Thousand Miles

Twenty Aircraft Take Off Separately

Speed and Obstacle Categories, Let's See Who Wins the Championship

(London) Twenty aircraft representing six countries departed from Mildenhall Aerodrome today for New Gold Mountain in Australia, marking the largest air race in history. Each aircraft took off at intervals of approximately one minute. The first aircraft took off at 6:30 AM, and the last aircraft left the ground at 6:47 AM. All aircraft flew directly towards Australia. Three aircraft competed in the speed race, ten aircraft competed in the speed and obstacle race, and seven aircraft competed in the obstacle race. The United Kingdom participated with six aircraft, the United States with three aircraft, the Netherlands with two aircraft, Australia with two aircraft, New Zealand with two aircraft, New Guinea and Denmark with one aircraft each. The Irish monoplane was disqualified due to being overweight. (National Telegram, 20th)

Aircraft Departure Situation 36

(Mildenhall) The air race was held here at 6:30 this morning. At that time, there were twenty aircraft, departing from England for Melbourne, each determined to break the previous record of flying 11,300 miles. By four in the morning, there were already thousands of spectators at the airfield. Mr. and Mrs. Mollison departed first amidst cheers. Subsequently, an aircraft took off every forty-five seconds, so within seventeen minutes, all twenty aircraft had completely left the departure point. Sir Powel, representing the Lord Mayor of London, was the flag bearer, holding a red flag and standing in the field. The pilot of the fifth aircraft, Stack and Tennler, failed to take off immediately after the red flag was raised and returned to the starting line, thus losing thirteen and a half minutes. It was later learned that Stack and others intended to return to take the photos taken at the time of departure and carry them to Melbourne in the aircraft. The Dutch aircraft took off after a short taxi, like a bird. However, the British aircraft Comet took off a little unevenly, and when the wheels left the ground, the fuselage almost reached the edge of the airfield. The aircraft Vega, piloted by Miller and Huch, was the twelfth to depart, due to a misunderstanding of the signal, taking off ten seconds early. They thought they could depart when the flag was raised, but they didn't know they had to fly when the flag was lowered. This error will be corrected in Singapore, but it does not contain any penalty. Most of the participants will make their first landing in Marseille. In addition, some plan to make their first landing in Rome, Bucharest (the capital of Romania), Baghdad, and Athens. The weather was overcast this morning, and visibility was normal, but the weather in the English Channel is expected to be good. However, the weather in continental Europe is not very good and will only improve when it reaches Turkey and Asia Minor. From four in the morning, people from all directions came to Mildenhall Airfield in an endless stream, like water flowing into a ravine. Men and women wore evening dresses, singing and dancing in the field to pass the time. The air was filled with joy, because in a moment there will be a great spectacle to feast their eyes. (Reuters Dispatch, 20th)

Four Aircraft Land En Route 37

(London) After the aircraft of the England-Australia Air Race departed from Mildenhall Aerodrome at dawn today, four aircraft had landed in France, either due to bad weather or engine damage. The rest proceeded smoothly. The aircraft that flew the farthest today was the Douglas DC-2 aircraft piloted by Parmentier and Moll of the Netherlands, which landed in Rome at 11:30 AM, exactly five hours from the time of departure. Several aircraft also passed through the Marseille checkpoint in the morning. The aircraft piloted by Stack and Tennler landed in the town of Abbeville near the mouth of the Somme River in northern France, sixty miles from Calais. According to Stack, they had to land due to heavy fog and now hope to continue after refueling. The remaining three aircraft landed in a small town near Paris, one landed in Beaujolais, and one landed near Beaujolais, but all hope to continue flying as soon as possible. The first aircraft to pass Marseille today was Vega, which landed at 10:24 AM and took off again at 10:50 AM. Another two aircraft, one landed in Marseille at 11:15 AM and resumed after thirty minutes, and one landed in Marseille at 12:08 PM. One American aircraft stopped briefly in Lyon at 11:05 AM. (Reuters Dispatch, 20th)

Dutch Aircraft Flies Over Athens 38

(London) The Dutch aircraft Douglas DC-2 has flown over Athens at 2:15 PM. Three of the four aircraft that were forced to land in France have resumed their journey. (Reuters Dispatch, 20th)

Irish City Temporarily Withdraws from the Race 39

Colonel Fitzmaurice, recommended by the Irish Hospital Trust Society, suddenly withdrew from the competition because the inspectors only allowed his aircraft to carry 5,400 pounds, while Fitzmaurice insisted on carrying 8,000 pounds. Because his request was not fulfilled, he announced his withdrawal, which surprised everyone. Everyone thought that Fitzmaurice had completed all the preparations for the competition and might fly to Australia alone to compete with the other aircraft.

(London) An Irish aircraft withdrew from the England-Australia air race due to a dispute over the amount of weight carried. According to the pilot, Colonel Fitzmaurice, he does not care about the 10,000-pound prize, but he is willing to demonstrate the capabilities of his aircraft. He now plans to take the aircraft to the Croydon Aerodrome for a landing test. After obtaining a certificate, he will fly to Australia as a private individual, taking the same route as the competitors, in order to beat the winner's time. He now hopes to depart on Sunday and take the route of the competitors to beat the winner's time. (Reuters Dispatch, 20th)

The King and Queen Visit the Field 40

Yesterday, the King and Queen suddenly visited Mildenhall Aerodrome, which greatly delighted the competitors, who welcomed them with joy. When the Queen spoke with Mrs. Mollison, also known as Amy Johnson, she asked her to carry a letter to the Duke of Gloucester, who is currently in Melbourne, Australia. The King and Queen inspected the aircraft with great interest and stayed in the field for more than half an hour. The Queen boarded the Royal Dutch large aircraft, which was her first time entering an aircraft. The Crown Prince and others drove an aircraft from Windsor to the field, inspected the aircraft for an hour and a half, and watched the competitor Wright perform aerial acrobatics in the sky with great joy. The Aviation Minister, Lord Londonderry, also arrived at the field by aircraft, inspected the field for a week, and chatted with the competitors happily. In addition, journalists, newspaper photographers, and newsreel photographers were specially allowed to enter the field to observe.

Prize Distribution Method 41

(London) The England-Australia air speed and obstacle race is named the MacRobertson International Air Race. Sir MacRobertson is a well-known citizen of Melbourne and has donated 15,000 pounds to the competition. There is also a gold trophy. The flight distance is 11,323 miles and must be completed in sixteen days. The first place will be awarded 10,000 pounds and a gold cup worth over 500 pounds. The second place will be awarded 1,500 pounds, and the third place will be awarded 500 pounds. The first place in the obstacle race will be awarded 2,000 pounds, and the second place will be awarded 1,000 pounds. Participants in the speed race must land at the following five locations for inspection: Baghdad (2,552 miles from London to Baghdad), Allahabad (2,300 miles from Baghdad to Allahabad), Singapore (2,210 miles from Allahabad to Singapore), Darwin (1,084 miles from Singapore to Darwin), and Charleville (1,389 miles from Darwin to Charleville), for a total of five stations. (The distance from Charleville to the Melbourne finish line is 787 miles).

Obstacle Race Regulations 42

The obstacle race regulations are: (1) The obstacle race course is the same as the speed race, but the obstacle race is determined by the fastest obstacle time. (2) The so-called obstacle time refers to the flight time minus the allowed obstacle time. The so-called flight time refers to the time spent from departure from London to the Melbourne finish line, and the inspection time at each station is not included in the flight time. (3) Obstacle inspection stations are set up approximately 500 miles apart. (Reuters Dispatch, 20th)

Italian Aviators Set New Water Flight Record 43

(Rome) Italian aviators Stefanini and Corrado flew a seaplane for 4,122 kilometers in 26 hours, breaking the world record set by American naval aviators McKennis and Fischer. The aircraft flown by Stefanini and Corrado was mass-produced and only had one engine with 750 horsepower. The maximum speed was 260 kilometers per hour, and the long-distance flight speed was 220 kilometers per hour. This aircraft will soon be used for long-range maritime reconnaissance. (Havas Dispatch, 19th)

Death of German General Kluck 45

Repeatedly Made Outstanding Achievements in the European War

(Berlin) German General Alexander von Kluck, who repeatedly made outstanding achievements in the European War, died of illness in the German capital this morning at the age of eighty-eight. General Kluck participated in the Austro-Prussian War in 1866 and later participated in the Franco-Prussian War from 1870 to 1871. He had a long military career and endured many battles. When the European War began, he was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the German First Army on the Western Front, responsible for offensive and defensive duties on the right wing. After winning consecutive victories in Maubeuge and Saint-Quentin, he personally led a large army to set out for Paris. This was one of the most thrilling events in the history of the European War. At that time, the German army was only twenty miles from Paris. If it were not for the Battle of the Marne, which stopped the German advance, the French capital would have become rubble. Later, Kluck's army retreated to the Aisne River defense line. He was seriously injured while inspecting the front-line trenches in March 1915. In October 1916, Kluck was unable to perform his arduous duties due to his declining health and retired. He wrote a book entitled "The March on Paris and the Battle of the Marne," which is a valuable historical material of the European War. The following is a record of his life and achievements: General Alexander von Kluck was born on May 21, 1848, in the city of Münster in Westphalia. His father was a public architect in the area. After graduating from school, he joined the 55th Infantry Brigade as a junior officer. In 1866, he followed General Vogel von Falkenstein to the Inn River. From 1870 to 1871, he participated in the Franco-Prussian War and was wounded twice near Metz, receiving the Iron Cross. Later, he was appreciated by Kaiser Wilhelm II and became the commander-in-chief of the Berlin Militia District. In 1909, he was awarded the title of baron and became a member of the nobility. Subsequently, he served as the commander of the 34th Brigade, the commander of the 23rd Army Corps, and the commander of the 37th Division. Later, he was promoted to the commander-in-chief of the 1st Guards Infantry Division. In 1913, he was appointed as the inspector of the 8th Army District. In the European War, he led the First Division to advance rapidly westward. He encountered the French army in Mons and won a great victory. Later, he defeated the British army in Saint-Quentin. In the Battle of the Marne, the enemy army, under the command of General Gallieni, planned to make a large encirclement, but Kluck unexpectedly broke through the encirclement by attacking against the besieged city. However, on the Aisne River front, he was injured by shrapnel and became chronically ill, eventually having to retire. In 1928, the University of Jena awarded him an honorary doctorate. In 1924, for his golden wedding anniversary, such a meritorious military figure, with such a long life, followed Hindenburg underground, which can be said to be an honor. (National Telegram, 19th)

League of Nations Special Assembly 46

Convened on November 20

Discuss the Gran Chaco Dispute

(Geneva) The Extraordinary Assembly of the League of Nations is now scheduled to convene on November 20 to discuss the Gran Chaco dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia in South America. (Havas Dispatch, 19th)

People's Militia of Three Counties Surrounded Bandits in Niulanshan 47

Wei Yonghe's Security Team Dispatched

(Tianjin) On the 19th, 150 bandits suddenly appeared in Tong County, fully armed and equipped with a mountain gun. After being intercepted by the local security team, the bandits were unable to enter the county and turned back, fleeing towards the border between Miyun and Shunyi. Along the way, they looted various villages, set fire to and destroyed many houses, and kidnapped dozens of men and women. The police and militia made every effort to pursue them, and the bandits fled again to Niulanshan in Shunyi County, resisting stubbornly by relying on the terrain. The people's militia of the three counties of Miyun, Shunyi, and Huairou have launched a large-scale encirclement and suppression, surrounding the bandits in the mountains. On the 19th, another 100 bandits passed through the border between Huairou and Miyun and fled into Pinggu County. The people's militia of Miyun and Pinggu counties divided their forces to intercept them, and the bandits fled back to Hanxinzhuang in Huairou, passing along the Bai River, Luoshan, Daxinzhuang, and Liushuizhuang, all of which were burned and looted severely. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

(Tianjin) The bandits in the war zone continue to cause disturbances in various counties. The entire force of Wei Yonghe's security Third General Team was dispatched, divided into teams to suppress bandits in Huairou, Miyun, Zunhua, and Jixian. Several hundred bandits who recently fled into Huairou were forced to flee to Luanping due to the intense pursuit by the people's militia. Another hundred or so fled to Qianfengkou on the Great Wall line. Xu Shiying, the commander of the Second Security Battalion, recently led some of his forces to suppress them in separate directions. (Special Dispatch, 20th)

Three Criminals in the Yutian Gongyue Case Escorted to Tianjin 48

(Tianjin) Wang Qinghong, the murderer in the Yutian Gongyue incident, and the wife's elder brother of the main culprit Wu Runbi, and two others were escorted to Tianjin from Ping today. Tax Police Crackdown on Illegal Salt Causes Tragedy in Luan County 49

(Tianjin) Salt is everywhere in the three counties of Luan County, Fengrun, and Leting, and the people mostly make a living by boiling salt. Recently, the tax police have been cracking down on illegal salt very severely, and conflicts have occurred from time to time. Afterwards, they were either resolved through mediation or sent to court, fortunately without escalation. Recently, due to the tragedy in Zhengjiawan, Luan County, the people's hatred of the tax police has become even more intense. More than a hundred tax police were stationed in Zhengjiawan. A few days ago, they learned that Zheng was making a living from a salt field and arrested Zheng. The people of the area believed that Zheng was not a salt bandit and went to the team to petition. The team released Zheng, and the people gathered outside the door again, shouting slogans. The tax police opened fire to suppress them, and the order was greatly disrupted. Two people died and five were injured. Afterwards, various villages received reports and united more than 2,000 people, heading straight for the team. The tax police were afraid that the situation would escalate and had no choice but to withdraw and telegraph the security team, saying that it was a riot by the villagers and asking them to come and suppress it. The security team rushed to the scene the next day and began to quell the situation. The villagers are now accusing the tax police at the Salt Transportation Office and various agencies, demanding that the murderers be punished. The Luan County Local Court is currently resolving the matter in accordance with the law. The two tax police who caused the incident have also been sent to court for detention pending trial. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 20th)

The Bandits on the Borders of Jiangxi and Fujian Are at the End of Their Rope 50

Complete Recovery Possible Within Two Months

(Xiamen) A military official in charge spoke to a Central News Agency reporter, stating that with the successive capture of Shicheng, Ruijin, and Xingguo, the bandits have no foothold on the borders of Jiangxi and Fujian. Within two months, the entire bandit area can be recovered. Only an empty city remains in Changting. There will be no problem for the Eastern Route Army to enter and garrison. However, because the bandits are implementing a scorched earth policy against us, our army must first prepare a sufficient supply of rice. Currently, after the vanguard advances to Hetian, they are engaged in urgently building rear highways. Once the road is open and transportation is smooth, they will advance further into Changting. The Jiangxi bandits are at the end of their rope and can be completely annihilated. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

(Nanchang) Xingguo reports that the bandits, in their desperate struggle, retreated entirely south of the Xingguo River after losing Xingguo. The people in the city were all coerced and taken away by the bandits. We are handling the aftermath, and those returning are enthusiastic. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

(Nanchang) Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Lu, arrived in Shicheng and agreed with Commander-in-Chief Chen on various matters concerning the aftermath: (1) Commander-in-Chief Chen will earnestly maintain military discipline and public morals to stabilize society; (2) Funds for resettlement and recruitment will be allocated by the province and will not be taken from local areas; (3) The corpses of bandits are scattered everywhere and the Department of Health will handle sanitation; (4) Emergency relief will be handled by the provincial relief committee. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

Ministry of Interior Explains Doubts Regarding the Regulations on Autonomous Districts, Townships, and Towns 51

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior explained two points of doubt regarding the execution of the regulations on autonomous districts, townships, and towns: (1) Trampling on other people's fields falls within the scope of civil mediation. The mediation committee of the district, township, or town can mediate according to the law. As for punishment, whether it be a fine or labor service, it concerns the people's property and bodily freedom. The head of the district, township, or town has no right to execute it directly. (2) As for loafers and idlers, they can be persuaded, but the head of the district, township, or town does not have the power to order them to work. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

Ministry of Industry Orders Provincial and Municipal Governments to Effectively Implement Factory Inspections 55

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry investigated the explosion at the Shanghai Taiyi Malt Essence Factory, which resulted in the death and injury of workers, stating that there was a lack of safety equipment. If the competent authorities had discovered it beforehand and ordered the factory to pay attention, this incident would not have occurred. However, there are many factories in various places, and safety equipment is extremely important. It specifically ordered the provincial and municipal governments to instruct factories to learn from the Shanghai Taiyi Factory and pay attention to improvements to avoid repeating the same mistakes. It also ordered the competent authorities to effectively implement factory inspections. If any factory has poor equipment, it should be enforced according to the law to ensure safety. The main point of the speech was that we should have the perseverance to study everything and should not have a perfunctory attitude. His language was humorous, and the audience laughed heartily. He later gave a speech at the Provincial Hospital and returned to Nanjing in the evening. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

Most of the Zhejiang Province Highway is Completed 106

(Hangzhou) Zhu Yaoting, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, returned to the province after inspecting the highways in the Taizhou, Wenzhou, and Chu prefectures. According to him, the provincial highway network is largely complete. However, the cost of ferries across the Lingjiang, Yongningjiang, Shuizhangjiang, and Qingjiang rivers along various sections is very high. If bridges can be built, it will take nine hours to go from Hangzhou to Wenzhou, and there is currently a need for twelve hours. This is already much more convenient than waterways. The total length of highways currently open to traffic is 3,400 kilometers. (Special dispatch on the 20th)

(Hangzhou) The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Joint Silk Factory Guidance Committee, organized by the National Economic Committee Silk Improvement Association, held its establishment meeting in Hangzhou. A Record of Inspecting the Northwest, by Our Special Correspondent Geng Ya

Gansu Province Construction Projects 109

Gansu Province's construction projects are in urgent need of active implementation. Areas like water conservancy, transportation, mining, and land reclamation all require substantial resources to effectively develop the province's strength. However, considering Gansu's finances, the vast expenses of military and political affairs, and the long-standing deficits in the provincial treasury, it is difficult to develop these construction projects sufficiently. As the province is a key center in the Northwest, critical for national defense, the central government, with foresight, urgently needs to develop the Northwest and provide assistance for construction. This is a crucial task. The past and present situation, and future plans for Gansu's construction projects are described as follows:

Lanzhou City is the capital of Gansu Province and is located in the center of the country. Its population is increasing year by year. According to a recent survey by the Public Security Bureau, there are a total of 19,773 households, with 96,009 people, including 59,990 males and 36,019 females. However, due to traffic congestion, various aspects are relatively backward. The Eurasian airline route has just established a station here, and the province's six major highway project also takes this place as its center. Land and air transportation are expected to gradually develop. Therefore, improving city roads and rectifying the city appearance are urgently needed. The Construction Department's recent plan for repairing and constructing city roads is roughly as follows: (1) Road system: The existing streets will be widened selectively, creating a grid layout, and as many radiating lines as possible will be added within a possible range to expand outward from the center. The main lines are planned to be developed in four directions, using the square at the north entrance of Zhongshan Avenue as the center: east to the Great Drill Ground, west to Xiaoxihu Lake, south to Wuquan Mountain, and north to the south bank of the Yellow River, connecting with the Gansu-Shaanxi highway main line via the Nan Guan and Dong Guan main streets, reaching the airport. In addition, branch lines will be appropriately opened to serve as connections. (2) Engineering plan: The principle is to use locally sourced materials. Bricks and stones produced in the city can be used for the entire foundation. Strip bricks and rectangular small stone strips are the best materials for paving sidewalks and express lanes. However, limited by economics, crushed mountain stone is used for the pavement. Open ditches will be built on both sides of the driveway to drain sewage. The main and branch lines of the city are 43 kilometers long, requiring a total estimated construction cost of 1,077,200 yuan. In addition, a private water company is being planned and discussed along the river.

Gansu Province has a woolen mill, originally called the Woolen Fabric General Bureau, which was established by Zuo Zongtang, the governor of Gansu, in the early years of the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty. The initial investment was 2 million taels of silver. Later, Peng Yingjia, the Lan Shan Daofu, continued to run it. Due to poor production and excessive expenses, it gradually became deficit-ridden and eventually closed down. Later, local gentry, such as Deng Long, raised funds to organize a joint public-private venture, renamed the Woolen Fabric Company. However, without effective reorganization methods, it soon closed down again. In the 15th year of the Republic of China, the provincial government took it back to continue running it, but production and sales were not developed. By the 19th year, it was closed again, and the factory's machinery was transferred to the Construction Department for safekeeping. In April of the 20th year, the provincial government planned to allocate funds to restore it, but it ultimately failed due to the provincial treasury's financial constraints. In the 21st year, the Construction Department drafted a method of attracting merchants for joint operation, but due to the impact of local finance, wealthy merchants did not dare to invest, causing the factory's vitality to be completely lost and restoration was difficult. Now, the Construction Department believes that the restoration of the woolen mill is essential, considering the province's flourishing animal husbandry and abundant wool production. Recently, in addition to requesting the provincial government to allocate funds for its restoration, it has also assigned technicians to supervise craftsmen to repair the machinery so that it can be restored as soon as possible to revitalize the industry.

Transportation is the beginning of all construction. Therefore, the development of the Northwest is generally considered to focus on transportation. Gansu's transportation has always been blocked, causing all industries to lag behind. In order to actively promote construction, the authorities first drafted a plan to build highways throughout the province, divided into six major lines: 1) Gansu-Shaanxi Line: from Gao Lan through Yu, Dingxi, Jingning, Longde, Pingliang, Jingchuan to Yaodian; 2) Gansu-Xinjiang Line: from Gao Lan through Yongdeng, Gulang, Wuwei, Yongchang, Shandan, Zhangye, Linze, Gaotai, Jiuquan, Yumen, Anxi to Xingxingxia; 3) Gansu-Qinghai Line: from Gao Lan to Xiangtang; 4) Gansu-Ningxia Line: from Gao Lan through Jingyuan to Zhongwei; 5) Gansu-Sichuan First Main Line: from Gao Lan along the Gansu-Shaanxi Line's Mengjiabao through Tongwei, Qin'an, Tianshui, Chengxian to Chengdu; 6) Gansu-Shaanxi Second Main Line: from Gao Lan through Tao Sha, Lintan, Minxian, Xigu, Wudu to Bikou, etc. Currently, only the roads from Lanzhou to Xi'an, to Xining, to Anxi, and to Ningxia are barely passable by cars. The rest are nominally borrowing cart roads and urgently need fundamental construction.

Gansu Province is located in the upper reaches of the Yellow River, with vast land. However, due to the arid highlands, there is no way to irrigate, and the desert extends for thousands of miles, making remediation difficult. Gansu Province has over 6 million people, and farmers account for 80-90% of the population. It is no wonder that these innocent people often experience drought. The solution is to dredge canals, manage ditches, and enable elevated land to receive irrigation. In this way, barren land will become fertile, people's livelihoods will be resolved, and it will also benefit the future management of the Yellow River. The general situation of water conservancy in Gansu Province is described as follows:

(1) Rainfall: Gansu's climate is dry and droughts are frequent. Although there are no precise measurements of annual rainfall, according to recent surveys, the middle area has about 18 inches (Lanzhou's annual rainfall is only about 11 inches according to actual measurements), the eastern area about 15 inches, the southern area about 20 inches, and the western area about 16 inches. However, the person in charge of the Lanzhou Tianzhu, entrusted by the Shanghai Xujiahui Observatory to conduct weather observations, said that the average annual rainfall in Gansu is only three inches (note: a normal rainfall of less than 18 inches cannot result in a good harvest and requires irrigation). Its inadequacy for farmland is obvious. If water conservancy irrigation and afforestation are not carried out to regulate the climate and increase rainfall, Gansu's farmland will undoubtedly become barren.

(2) Rivers: All major rivers north of the Yangtze River pass through Gansu Province, such as the Yellow River, Jing, Wei, Tao, Han, Zhang, Rui, Dang, Sha, Qingshui, Heishui, Datong, Zhuangdu, Longtan, Shule, Lin, Guo, Baiting, Huanjiang, Dong, Bei, Zhusha, as well as the Jialing, Bailong, and Liangjiang rivers, crisscrossing like a spider web. However, the water flow is rapid, making it difficult to open canals for irrigation. Therefore, the remains of garrison farmland canals from the Qin and Han dynasties can be found everywhere.

(3) Waterwheels: In nearby counties of Gansu Province, waterwheels are occasionally built as tools for drawing water for irrigation. However, they require a lot of effort and have little effect. The current number of waterwheels in each county is: Yongjing 53, irrigating 9,639 mu; Jingyuan 24, irrigating 10,800 mu; Gaolan 176, irrigating 29,710 mu; Taosha 1, irrigating 100 mu, totaling 254, irrigating 50,249 mu.

(4) Completed canals: Lintao County has 12 canals, including Deyuan, Gongzhen, Yongning, Fumin, Xinmin, Tao Hui, Liulin, Haoshui, Jiehe, Gaihe, Bayang, and Cuiwan. Tianyong County only has Tonghui Canal, which opens a canal at the Shangxiakou Nanwan of the county, leading the Wei River to the Shangxiakou Heiyaowan, which is 6,000 meters long, irrigating more than 1,000 mu. Other counties, due to the names of the canals are not detailed, the total number of completed canals in the province is about 170, irrigating about 2 million mu.

(5) Unfinished canals: Lintao County has four canals, including Puji, Jisheng, Mona, and Dongyu. Yongjing County has canals such as Yongfengchuan and Lamachuan. When these two counties' unfinished canals are completed in the future, they can irrigate more than 90,000 mu of farmland.

(6) Proposed canals: Lintao County has canals such as Minsheng and Anchuan. Gaolan has canals such as Xingu and Dajiachuan. Wuwei has canals such as Tao La, Yan Gan, and Er He. Longxi County has Longxi South Canal. Jingtai has Heimaquan River Canal. Yongdeng has Honggucheng Canal. Pingliang has Pingliangchuan Canal. There are Jinghe and Ji He canals in Chuan. Tianshui has the Weihe River Dike, guiding the Longhe River. Jingning has Kushui River Canal. If all the unfinished and proposed canals in the above counties can be completed, the total estimated project cost will be 1.7 million yuan, and it can irrigate more than 600,000 mu of farmland. Calculating an increase of three yuan per mu per year, the total annual income of farmers will be more than 2 million yuan. For this rural economy, which is increasingly declining, it is no different from obtaining a good medicine for revival and restoring its prosperity.

Autumn Floods in Guilin Become a Disaster 110

Flooding in Guilin Rivers Causes Severe Disaster

Flooding in Rivers of Western Guangdong

Guangzhou dispatch: Since the beginning of autumn, there has been more rain than sunshine in various parts of Guilin Province. At the beginning of this month, there were even hurricanes and rainstorms, and the water levels of the rivers rose simultaneously. In the Nanning area of Guilin Province, on the night of the 2nd of this month, the weather changed suddenly, with hurricanes and heavy rain. Mountain floods broke out in various counties. The most severe were the following counties: Longzhou: On the morning of the 2nd, there was torrential rain, lasting for several days and nights. The river water rose to 26 feet. Shangsi County: Heavy rain on the 2nd, non-stop throughout the night. Many houses of residents near the city collapsed, and fields were washed away. Long'an County: Wind and rain on the 2nd and 3rd, non-stop all day. The river water rose by three meters. Xunzhou: The upper and southern rivers both rose by nine feet four inches. Yujiang River: From the 2nd to the 4th, the water rose by eight meters and two centimeters. On the 6th, it continued to rise by eight centimeters. Beiliu River: The water level suddenly rose by four feet on the 3rd, three feet on the 4th, and one foot on the 5th. Dahe River: The water rose by one foot on the 3rd, three feet on the 4th, and three feet five inches on the 5th. Mingjiang River: The water rose by three zhang four chi on the 3rd, and five feet again on the 4th. Fields near the county seat and in the Zhaian Township area were all flooded, and the autumn harvest was hopeless. More than 200 rural power poles were uprooted. Ningming County: From the 1st to the 2nd, there were gales and heavy rain, lasting for two days and nights. Trees were uprooted and houses collapsed everywhere. Newly built public offices and school buildings in various villages of Kuitang Township collapsed. The autumn harvest is hopeless. The above-mentioned disasters in various counties are unprecedented in the past ten years. Yesterday, the Wuzhou Civil Aviation Airport was also flooded, and the Southwest Civil Aviation planes have been grounded for several days.

After the inundation of various places along the river in Guilin Province, the West River in Guangdong Province, originally the tail of the Guijiang River, has been receiving floodwaters flowing eastward from Guilin Province in recent days. The first to suffer are the counties of Gao Yao, Gao Ming, De Qing, and San Shui. The enclosure management committees of the above-mentioned counties immediately convened an emergency meeting to discuss ways to rescue the embankments. It was resolved that on the 16th of this month, the Gao Yao Gao Ming Thirteen Enclosure Flood Prevention Committee would be established to actively handle flood prevention work. Unfortunately, from the 8th to the 13th, the lower reaches of the West River were again subjected to continuous wind and rain. The wind aided the water's force, so the counties from Deqing to Sanshui became a vast flood. Gao Ming County suffered the most severe disaster. The San Zhou enclosure under the county's jurisdiction has been flooded, and the embankment is in imminent danger. All rice fields have been submerged in the water. On the evening of the 12th, the flood flooded to the southeast gate of the county seat, and the suburbs became a swamp. In addition to leading personnel to find ways to prevent flooding, the county magistrate urgently telegraphed the River Management Association, requesting that engineers be sent to the county to jointly rescue the dangerous embankments. (October 15th)

Henan Province Expands Long-Distance Telephone Service 111

This Year Adds Zhengzhou-Xuchang, Shangye, Yanwu Lines

Kaifeng dispatch: Henan Province's long-distance telephone service has been gradually set up in recent years with the stability of the political situation and the pacification of banditry. By the end of last year, there were 59 trunk and branch lines, totaling more than 8,230 li in length. According to the director of the bureau, Yu Zehou, this year the Zhengzhou-Xuchang line has been erected and repaired, the Shangye line completed, and the Yanwu, Xinwu, and Nanxi lines have been added. The details are as follows:

Zhengzhou-Xuchang Line: Originally, there was a telephone line between Kaifeng and Xuchang, with a length of 180 li, but it was attached to telegraph poles. Because the inductive force between the two lines was very strong, the sound of the call was often mixed. In addition, the telegraph bureau was urging to move the line, so new poles were re-erected according to the original line, and new lines were re-hung to avoid the problem of mixed sound. The bureau dispatched the director of the Zhengzhou branch, Guo Jingqi, to lead the work on March 1 of this year. By March 16, the entire line was completed. Since the call was made, it has been exceptionally clear.

Shangye Line: Shangcheng to Yejiaji, a distance of 140 Huali, was dispatched to Huangchuan branch director Liu Shancheng in November of the 22nd to lead the work erection. The project started from the 30th of that month to December 15 erected to Wumiao set. Because of the bandit, the project was suspended in the middle. It was not until March 6 of this year that the erection continued. The entire line was completed to March 20, but it is difficult to maintain in that area. According to a recent report, the line was destroyed again by the bandits.

Yanwu Line: From Luohe (i.e., Yancheng) through Wuyang to Ye County, the mileage is 160 li. The required material funds for the original long-distance telephone were apportioned equally according to the number of miles in each county, but because the material funds that Ye County should have apportioned have not been paid, the bureau sent Zhang Zengrong, director of the Kaifeng Nanguan Business Office, to lead the work on June 6 of this year. The section from Yancheng to Wuyang will be set up first. By June 15, the line was completed and the call began. Once Ye County turns over the required apportioned money, the entire line of Yanwu Ye can continue to be erected to complete it.

Xinwu Line: Xinyang to Wusheng Pass is a distance of 105 Huali. South of Wusheng Pass, it enters Hubei Province. In order to complete the Henan-Hubei combined line to facilitate communication, a clerk, Xie Shaozhen, was dispatched in June of this year to lead the work. The erection started on the 14th of that month, and the entire line was completed on July 2. It is connected to Guangshui. Now, Xinyang and Hankou can talk directly.

Nanxi Line: The erection of the Nanyang-Zhenping-Neixiang-Xichuan long-distance telephone is necessary for bandit, so as to connect with Yun County in Hubei Province so that the news can be well informed. In addition to the Nanyang-Zhenping section, the bureau had originally erected a line. From Zhenping to Neixiang, it is ninety Huali; from Neixiang to Xichuan, it is 140 Huali. Because it is necessary to connect with Yun County, it was erected to the small Sailing, the border of this province, after reaching Xichuan. There are forty Huali. The bureau sent Zhang Zengrong, director of the Kaifeng Nanguan Business Office, to lead the work on July 22 of this year, and it was completed on September 13. Because the internal line in Yun County, Hubei Province, has not yet been erected, the joint call between the two provinces still needs to be waited for. (18th)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Approves Rules for Smokers to Quit Smoking 112

Rehabilitating Smokers are Divided into Three Classes for Fees

No Request to Go Out Midway Unless Completely Abandoned

Zhenjiang dispatch: After the deadline for the general registration of smokers in Jiangsu Province, drug rehabilitation hospitals in various counties have been successively established one after another. The Provincial Anti-Smoking Association regards urging smokers to quit smoking as the most important task in anti-smoking. It has specially formulated the Jiangsu Province Smokers' Smoking Cessation Rules, which has been passed by the provincial government meeting and issued to all counties for promulgation and implementation. The details are as follows: "Article 1 of the Jiangsu Province Smokers' Smoking Cessation Rules: These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 2 of the Jiangsu Province Drug Rehabilitation Hospital Organization Regulations and Article 2 of the Jiangsu Province Drug Rehabilitation Organization Regulations for Each County (hereinafter referred to as Drug Rehabilitation Hospitals). Article 3: Any smoker in the province who has one of the following circumstances may fill out a smoking cessation application and apply to the Anti-Smoking Committee for rehabilitation, or be issued by the Anti-Smoking Committee for rehabilitation: 1. Those who have applied to the County Anti-Smoking Committee to quit smoking during the general registration period; 2. Those who have been registered and licensed and have reached the smoking cessation period; 3. Those who have been registered and licensed but have not reached the smoking cessation period and voluntarily quit smoking in advance; 4. Relatives of smokers apply to drug rehabilitation hospitals for coercive rehabilitation (the form of the smoking cessation application will be determined separately). Article 4: All smokers who are rehabilitated must reside in a drug rehabilitation hospital. Article 5: The following fees shall be charged for smokers who are rehabilitated: 1. Smoking cessation fee: Category A: 20 yuan, Category B: 10 yuan, Category C: 2 yuan. Those who meet the circumstances of Article 3, Item 1 are exempt from the smoking cessation fee. 2. Food expenses: Category A: 40 cents per day, Category B: 20 cents per day, Category C: 10 cents per day. Ten days must be paid in advance when entering the hospital, and the remainder will be paid in installments. The above fees may be increased or decreased by the drug rehabilitation hospital depending on local circumstances, and a separate fee schedule will be submitted to the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee for approval. Article 6: Smokers who are rehabilitated shall abide by the smoking cessation rules (the smoking cessation rules shall be formulated by the drug rehabilitation hospital). Article 7: Smokers who are rehabilitated must live in separate wards for men and women. Article 8: Separate wards must be set up for those who voluntarily request to quit smoking and those who are issued for coercive rehabilitation. Article 9: Smokers shall be treated by a smoking cessation doctor during the rehabilitation period, but may not request to go out for medical treatment on this basis. Article 10: If a smoker dies due to illness during the rehabilitation period, the drug rehabilitation hospital shall report to the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee, and the County Drug Rehabilitation Center shall report to the County Anti-Smoking Committee, who shall send personnel to inspect it and hand it over to the relatives of the rehabilitated smoker for burial. Article 11: Smokers shall not request to go out midway unless they have completely quit smoking. Article 12: When a smoker quits smoking in the hospital and is certified by the doctor of the hospital that he has indeed quit smoking and is allowed to be discharged from the hospital, he shall find an guarantor, issue a guarantee that he will never smoke again, and be given a smoking cessation certificate by the drug rehabilitation hospital, the form of which will be determined separately. Article 13: When relatives of smokers send a request for coercive rehabilitation, the hospital shall notify the relatives of the smoker in advance and issue a guarantee before they can be taken back. Article 14: If a smoker applies for smoking cessation and the hospital ward cannot accommodate him at the time, he may register in advance and be notified to come for rehabilitation on schedule, or the hospital may submit a report to the provincial and county associations to temporarily designate public or private hospitals with registered and qualified doctors to rehabilitate him. Article 15: Smokers who have quit smoking in public or private hospitals or private clinics must still hold the certificate to find a guarantor and issue a guarantee to the Provincial Drug Rehabilitation Hospital or the County Drug Rehabilitation Center before they can exchange it for a hospital smoking cessation certificate. However, the Provincial and County Drug Rehabilitation Hospitals may refuse to issue or re-issue smoking cessation certificates after a conditional examination without addiction. Smokers who only hold a public or private hospital clinic smoking cessation certificate will not be effective. Article 16: All staff of the Provincial Drug Rehabilitation Hospital and the County Drug Rehabilitation Center at all levels, such as abuse, extortion, malfeasance, etc. to smokers in the hospital, will be severely punished according to law once reported and verified. Article 17: If there are any matters not covered in these rules, the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee may submit a report to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for revision. Article 18: These rules shall be promulgated and implemented by the Jiangsu Provincial Government after being passed by the Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee meeting (19th)

Songjiang County Government Convenes Autumn Survey Conference 113

The county's agricultural products are mainly rice and cotton, and farmers depend on them for their livelihood. The prosperity of industry and commerce is also based on the abundance of agricultural harvests. There was a severe drought in the summer of this year, and the rivers were dry and shallow. Farmers bucketed water day and night, working tirelessly and sufferingly, lamenting the worry of drought and famine. Fortunately, during the flowering and fruiting period in autumn, there were continuous showers, and the rice and cotton, which had been on the verge of extinction, began to recover. The county government previously received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs and Finance to investigate the famine, and instructed the district offices to survey and respond. After the two departments sent commissioners to re-survey, the county government convened district chiefs and relevant groups at 10:00 a.m. today (20th) to hold an autumn survey conference. The county magistrate presided over the meeting, and Wang, the commissioner of the Department of Civil Affairs, and Li, the commissioner of the Department of Finance, attended together, reporting the re-survey process. After discussion, except for the sixth and seventh districts, which had good harvests, the first, second, third, fourth, and fifth districts were generally reduced by 20%. The eighth district is a coastal area, and the famine is more severe. It is approved to generally reduce it by 60%. It is proposed to submit it to the provincial government for approval.

Son Suspected in Father's Death in the Field 114

Sun Lanqin, a farmer from Heyingtang, Fourteenth District, Fengjing, died suddenly in the field. His nephew, Songgen, reported it to his aunt, who reported it to the Second Branch, which reported it to the court for inspection. At that time, the deceased's son, Songpo, suddenly disappeared, and there was a suspicion of fratricide, or that father and son were killed at the same time. Yesterday, the court sent someone to inspect the body, and found that the deceased's temple was injured by bricks and stones, and there were fatal injuries on the chest and ribs. The blood flowed all over the ground, and the situation was terrible. It was learned that the deceased's daughter saw that her brother, Songpo, was stained with blood, suspected him, and reported it to her stepmother, who asked the Second Branch to arrest and escort Songpo to Songjiang. The county Public Security Bureau is now preparing a document to transfer him to the county court for interrogation.

Provisional Business Tax on Nanhui Cotton Begins 115

The Provincial Department of Finance sent Yu Peng to Nanhui the day before to assist the Chuanhui Feng Business Tax Bureau in actively handling the collection of the provisional business tax as the new cotton is on the market. Yesterday, the member visited County Magistrate Yuan to discuss the county's assistance procedures. The county ordered each district chief to notify provisional merchants, companies, and brokers that all purchases of cotton must pay business tax in accordance with the law, and may not resist. If anyone still fails to comply after the 12th of this month, the tax bureau will report it, and the police will be dispatched to pursue it.

Fifteen-Year-Old Villager in Taicang Kills with a Kitchen Knife 116

Yao Awu, a villager from the Shangliutu Village, Twelfth District, Huchuan Township, First District, is engaged in farming. The day before, he had a verbal quarrel with his neighbor, Chen Wu. Chen A Yu, the 15-year-old son of the woman, saw that Awu and his mother were arguing endlessly, so he took a kitchen knife from his own kitchen and slashed Awu in the head when he was unprepared. Suddenly, blood gushed out and he fell to the ground unconscious. The Huchuan Public Security Police Station, which is in charge of the area, arrested the murderer and sent him to the General Bureau along with Chen Wu and the injured person, and transferred him to the county government. The assessor Shen Cheng opened a criminal court to try the case, examined the wounds, ordered him to seek medical treatment outside, and the murderer Chen Axing was detained, and Chen Wu was released on bail pending further investigation.

Chairman of Suzhou South Association, Shi Junqing, Passes Away 117

Shi Junqing, chairman of the Wu County Chamber of Commerce and senior advisor to the Jiangsu Provincial Business Federation, served the community diligently and tirelessly. He died of illness due to overwork at 3:00 p.m. on the 18th. Yesterday afternoon, the funeral was held. The County Chamber of Commerce has notified all industries that the entire business community will lower the flag to half-mast for one day to express their condolences. The fire brigades in each district of Suzhou will each send a delegation of 20 members to pay their respects. After Shi Junqing's death, the County Chamber of Commerce immediately convened an emergency meeting and appointed Standing Committee Member Pan Ziqi as the acting chairman, and a by-election will be held at a later date. Shi Junqing started his career in the silk and satin industry. In recent years, due to the decline of the silk and satin industry, there have been annual losses, so his family's situation is not as good as it used to be.

Wuxi Telegraphs Request to Reduce Stamp Tax Rate 118

The County Chamber of Commerce of this county telegraphed the Nanjing Central Political Conference yesterday, requesting a reduction in the stamp tax rate, stating that the stamp tax law decided by the Legislative Yuan stipulates that invoices and money receipts of three yuan to ten yuan should be affixed with one point, and thereafter one point should be added for every ten yuan, up to a maximum of one yuan, which is a hundred times and fifty times higher compared with the current stamp tax regulations, which stipulate that invoices should be affixed with one point and all kinds of money receipts should be affixed with a maximum of two points. The fifth article of the principle of the stamp tax law passed by Junhui last year stipulates that "taxes should be levied heavily on documents with greater validity or rights, or longer usage time, and taxes should be levied lightly on documents with lesser validity or rights, or shorter usage time," and the sixth article stipulates that "commonly used documents should be taxed at a fixed tax rate that is simple and easy to implement, while documents for rare acts should be taxed at a progressive tax rate that is easy to calculate," which is obviously inconsistent. It is found that the validity period of merchants' invoices and receipts is extremely short, but the tax rate is increased by hundreds or fifty times compared with the current tax rate, and the books are also doubled compared with the previous ones, which merchants cannot afford. The principles decided last year should be quickly corrected.

Questionable Verification of a Smoker 119

Hua Juchu, the Chief of General Affairs at the local Tobacco and Alcohol Public Sales Inspection Office, had a long-standing addiction to opium and was a heavy smoker for over twenty years. When the county's anti-smoking association organized the registration and licensing of smokers, Hua did not register and obtain a license as required. Consequently, Wang Zuogeng, a vendor, reported him for privately smoking opium without a license, and he was brought to the Public Security Bureau, transferred to the county's anti-smoking association, and sent to the county's addiction treatment center for verification. As the center lacked the necessary equipment, an observational verification method was used, lasting seven days. During this period, Hua smoked cigarettes all day, chewed on pumpkin seeds until his mouth foamed, and consumed supplements such as "Chrysanthemum Brand" milk, cod liver oil, and ginseng, as well as pears, appearing extremely distressed, indicating signs of addiction. However, after the observation period, yesterday, the Director of the County Addiction Treatment Center, Gu Zengliang, reported that Hua showed no signs of addiction. Subsequently, Chairman Yan instructed Hua Hongtao, the Chief of the General Affairs Section of the anti-smoking association, to hold a hearing and rigorously interrogate Hua Juchu about his time at the center. Hua admitted to purchasing and consuming cigarettes and supplements. When questioned, the informant, Wang Zuogeng, insisted that Hua was a long-time addict and deemed the county addiction treatment center's verification inaccurate, declaring in court his intention to appeal to the provincial authorities for a re-examination of Hua's addiction. Consequently, Wang Zuogeng was temporarily detained, while Hua Juchu was released on bail with a reliable guarantor, pending referral to the provincial authorities for re-examination and handling. Hua Juchu's report was the first since the county's ban on smoking, making it a matter of significant public attention.

Jiangyin Prefectural Commissioners Arrive in Cheng for Disaster Assessment of Damaged Fields 120

This summer's severe drought resulted in a harvest of less than 40%. The total area of ​​disaster-stricken farmland in the county is more than 229,000 mu, which has been verified by the county government and reported to the provincial government. Yesterday (18th), Jin Langxi from the Civil Affairs Department, He Zhaoxi from the Construction Department, and Jiang Nanchun from the Finance Department came to Cheng to assess the disaster situation. After meeting with Secretary Bao of the County Government, it was decided that starting from the 19th, they would first inspect the townships under the first district, and then inspect the wasteland in each district. After returning to the provincial government, they will average the most and least severely affected fields in each district to determine the autumn harvest.

Changshu Drought Relief Association Borrows Funds to Provide Wheat Seeds 121

The Drought Relief Association held a meeting at the county government on the 19th. The participating committee members and district chiefs resolved the following important matters: (1) It was decided that the cotton fields in the eastern districts 2, 5, and 6 had suffered significant damage. A resolution was made to send a letter to each district chief to investigate the most severely affected farmers, compile a list and report it, and approve the lending of 2,000 shi of wheat seeds. (2) Yu Jiusi, Qu Liangshi, Pang Diancai, Wang Qianqi and others were designated to borrow 10,000 yuan from the bank, and 10,000 yuan was allocated from the preparedness fund to purchase wheat seeds for lending. This loan is secured by ten water pumping machines. (3) The previously purchased water pumping machines are now ineffective and should be collected from each district and entrusted to the agricultural farm for safekeeping and maintenance for future leasing. (4) Yu Jiusi, Zou Sicheng, and Pang Diancai were designated as representatives to attend the autumn harvest meeting.

Jiangsu Private Electricity Association Opens in Changshu 122

The 8th annual meeting of the National Private Electric Enterprise Association, Jiangsu Provincial Branch, is being held in Changshu. The local county electric plant and others are hosting it. The meeting is scheduled to be held at the Electric Plant on Xueqian Street for three days starting on the 21st. All expenses will be shared equally by the local county electric light plant, telephone company, and the Jiangyin Minghua Electric Plant. The meeting date has arrived, and the preparations have been completed. As for hosting representatives from various regions, it was originally hoped to borrow vehicles from the Xichang Road for transportation, but since the road has not yet been completed, separate reception points have been set up in Wuxi and Suzhou West. It is scheduled to travel to Changshu by boat on the 20th. A large number of representatives have come to Changshu this time, as many as more than 150 people, even representatives from Fuzhou have come to participate. In addition to setting up electric torch arches on the main thoroughfares, the association has also reserved 130 sedan chairs from various sedan chair shops for the representatives to tour Yushan. These rattan sedan chairs have all been reserved, and other tourists may miss out. In addition, the Construction Committee has also sent Xue Shaoqing, a technician and national electricity industry instructor, to Changshu to give instructions. The Construction Department has also telegraphed Zhai Huan, the county magistrate of this county, to participate nearby as a representative.

Zhenjiang Drought Relief Association Petitions Province 123

Zhenjiang suffered unusually heavy drought this summer, with more than 460,500 mu of land yielding no harvest, resulting in losses of more than 4.507 million yuan and affecting more than 148,800 people. Only a small part of the seven districts in the county were affected by the disaster, and the rest were devastated and yielded no harvest. The provincial government decided to allocate 30,000 yuan for work relief, which was far from sufficient. Yesterday, the Zhenjiang Drought Relief Conference decided to send seven groups, including the Zhenjiang County Party Headquarters, the County Chamber of Commerce, the Drought Relief Association, the Women's Association, the Farmers' Association, the Education Association, and the Journalists' Association, to petition the provincial government for an increase in funds. Because the chairman was not in the province, Secretary-General Luo received them on his behalf. After the representatives reported on the disaster situation in Zhenjiang, the Secretary-General promised to forward it to the chairman for review and instructions.

Excellent Results in Land Survey Reporting 124

The Zhenjiang County Government, upon receiving instructions from the Finance Department, conducted a land survey and reporting process, which began actively on March 10th of this year and was completed after two and a half months. Subsequently, they began to sort it out, first sorting out the survey reports submitted by each district according to the maps and grain areas, and then ordering the clerks to compare and calculate the grain maps and survey reports to serve as the basis for grain collection. It has now been checked and completed. The results show that there are a total of 32,356 mu, 6 fen, 8 li, 4 hao, and 3 si of excess taxable land and 6,063 mu, 7 fen, 3 li, 2 hao, 3 si, and 8 hu of reed fields, various fields, and beaches.

A Tragedy Occurs Due to Careless Gun Repair in Gaoyou 125

Wang Jinren, a farmer in Zhengjiadun, District 6 of this county, bought a self-defense gun last year, which had not been used for a long time. He took it out yesterday to repair it, and several bullets inside were not taken out. It went off accidentally, and the bullets pierced Wang's palm in several places. He immediately fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Fortunately, Chen Shufen, a patrol officer of the Provincial Public Security Team on the water, heard the sound and rushed to rescue him, and his life is not in danger.

Intense Gun Battle Between Police and Bandits in Haifu Town, Haimen 126

Haifu Town, District 6, is close to the coast. Yesterday (the 18th) at 9 p.m., more than 60 sea bandits suddenly landed with weapons, intending to rob. The police team of the Reclamation and Animal Husbandry Company and the 4th Squad of the Juyang Town Security Team rushed to intercept them. The two sides fought fiercely for more than 20 minutes, and the bandits gradually became unable to hold on and retreated one after another. After the county government learned about it, it sent a team to assist in the defense that night.

Hangzhou Fire Brigade Chief Dies in the Line of Duty 127

Sun Liansheng, a resident of No. 20 Shankou Lane outside the Genshan Gate of Hangzhou City, accidentally started a fire at 7 p.m. on the 19th due to careless cooking, and the accumulated firewood suddenly caught fire. The fire was quite fierce, and the fire brigade immediately dispatched fire trucks to put out the fire. It was completely extinguished in about half an hour. A total of six houses were burned down, with losses of about 2,000 yuan. However, Xi Jinlong, the commander of the third team of the fire brigade, suffocated in the flames on the spot due to his efforts to put out the fire and disregard for his own safety. After being rushed to the hospital by the team members, he died of a heart hemorrhage at 9 p.m. The entire team plans to hold a memorial service to express their grief.

Retrial Verdict in the Xu Zhuoran Case 128

After the case of the assassination of Xu Zhuoran in Fujian was transferred to the Hangzhou Local Court for trial, the second instance of the High Court ruled that Ye Caizhen, Chen Yanxiang, Chen Delin, and Lin Min were not suspected of murder and were not guilty, and Lin Luo was sentenced to two years in prison. Later, because the prosecutor refused to accept the verdict, he appealed to the Supreme Court, which sent it back for retrial. Coincidentally, the Fujian Incident occurred, and the three people, Ye and others, could not be summoned. Only Lin Min, who was in custody, was questioned. The verdict was announced yesterday, rejecting the prosecutor's appeal.

Ningbo Zhishan Bandits Rob Four Homes in One Night 129

Liangjiao'ao, Zhishan Township, District 7 of Ningbo, is located on the coast and surrounded by the sea on three sides. It has always been a place where bandits hide. There are more than 100 households, most of whom are farmers. At about 12 o'clock the night before, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, broke into the home of Hu Xiaoquan, tied up Xiaoquan and his wife, and forced them to hand over silver dollars. Xiaoquan resisted slightly, and the bandits raised sharp knives and cut off the feet of Xiaoquan and his wife. Xiaoquan and his wife were unable to move due to pain, and they ransacked the boxes and cabinets and fled with their loot. Afterwards, it was reported to the police station in charge, and the police captured Zhang Baocai, Zhang Mingcong, Zhang Minghong, and three other suspects, who were sent to the county government for interrogation.

Local News

Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee Implements Exchange Rate Stabilization Yesterday 136

4-4-2 System for Fund Allocation

Ministry of Finance Subsidizes Operating Losses

According to Shen Shi News Agency, the Ministry of Finance, together with the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, established the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee. After concretely deciding on the principles the day before yesterday, all working steps have been decided after repeated secret talks between the three representatives, Bei Songsun, Xi Demao, and Zhang Peishen, since the evening of the day before yesterday. As this work has no fixed form and requires temporary and flexible response, it will be handled by the three parties through consultations at any time when it begins. The organization and detailed rules have been drafted by Bei Songsun and will be formally approved after being discussed again by the Central Bank and the Bank of Communications today. The committee's fund of 100 million yuan has been decided to be borne by the Central Bank and the Bank of China, each responsible for 40 million yuan, and the Bank of Communications responsible for 20 million yuan. Funds will be allocated to each bank at any time within the prescribed limits as needed. When necessary, the total amount of funds can be negotiated and adjusted at any time.

Ministry of Finance Bears Subsidy for Losses 137

This time, the banks formed the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee entirely under the supervision and entrustment of the Ministry of Finance. However, its operating activities are of an independent nature, and its work policy is also different from that of general commercial entities. Therefore, it will not hesitate to suffer losses under special circumstances in order to maintain market stability. However, the Ministry of Finance has agreed to subsidize these losses. According to the general inspection of the banking industry, it is said that if the foreign exchange balance work is handled properly, there will be no losses.

Main Functions of the Foreign Exchange Committee 138

According to a banker familiar with exchange rate trends who spoke to reporters yesterday morning, after the establishment of the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee, its main function is to stabilize the domestic silver market so that there will be no sudden rise or fall. That is, when the price of silver dollars falls, the Stabilization Committee will buy silver dollars and sell US dollars or shillings to raise the price of silver. Conversely, if silver dollars skyrocket, it will release silver dollars and buy US dollars and shillings to suppress the degree of the surge, in order to keep the silver market and exchange rate at an appropriate level. Another banker observed that it is expected that the government will lower the domestic currency price to a ratio of five to one with the US dollar in order to help the export of domestic products. However, it is feared that if the price of silver dollars suddenly plummets, our exporters will inevitably be disadvantaged. Therefore, the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee will be used to make it progress gradually and avoid special impacts.

China Commercial Bank Expresses Approval 139

The Ministry of Finance originally intended to include other China Commercial Banks in the organization of the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee, in addition to the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. Therefore, when Minister Kong convened a meeting the previous morning, Chen Guangfu of Shanghai Bank, Li Fusun of Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and others also participated in the discussion. Now, for some reason, the final decision was made to only organize the committee jointly by the Central Bank and the other two banks. According to the Shen Shi News Agency reporter's interview with leaders of various China Commercial Banks yesterday morning, they all expressed that although the private China Commercial Banks will be slightly affected in terms of foreign exchange business, they unanimously expressed their support for the government's approach, considering the overall Chinese financial market. They said that if the foreign exchange stabilization work can be carried out effectively, it is expected to achieve quite satisfactory results. Most foreign banks were unwilling to express any opinions.

Mark Gold Prices Rise, Balance Tax Drops 140

Since the increase in the silver export tax, the mark gold price has been greatly affected. The opening price yesterday morning at 9:00 was 980 yuan and 5 jiao. The lowest price fell to 976 yuan, and then rose to 990 yuan. The closing price at 12:00 noon was 999 yuan, an increase of 13 yuan compared to the closing price of 986 yuan the day before. The Central Bank's balance tax rate was listed yesterday morning with an additional balance tax of 10.25%, which was 0.25% lower than the day before. The balance tax rate the day before was 10.5%.

Financial Leaders Deny Rumors 141

Inflation is Not a Fact

Devaluation is Also Untrue

Since the Ministry of Finance increased the export tax on silver, prices have risen sharply, and transactions on various exchanges have been very active. On Thursday, the price of gold rose to 1,020 yuan, and other commodities such as yarn, flowers, flour, etc. also experienced huge price increases. However, when comparing the supply and demand of spot goods with the transactions in the market, it seems that the distance is still far. All this is due to rumors that my country will also devalue its currency, inflate the currency, or even switch to the gold standard, so they regard buying mark gold, foreign exchange, or other goods as a shortcut to getting rich, resulting in drastic changes in the market. After the newspapers published the statement of the person in charge of the Ministry of Finance on Friday, clarifying that the government would not abolish the silver standard or ban the export of silver, the rumors of abolishing silver and using gold were swept away. However, yesterday there were rumors that it was possible to devalue the currency to inflate the currency, causing anxiety again. The reporter asked a banker about this, and it was said that he had just met with financial leaders and inquired about this, and he now knew very well that there was absolutely no such thing as devaluing the currency or inflating the currency. Although there are many rumors these days, they are all speculations by general speculators and are not credible.

Huge Customs Revenue After Silver Tax Collection 142

A Total of More Than 200,000 Yuan

Paid by the Bank of the Netherlands

Since the Jianghai Customs was ordered to collect silver export tax, the bulk export of silver dollars by foreign banks in this port on the 16th has stopped and has been returned to each bank for storage. Only the Bank of the Netherlands still loaded a batch of silver for export after the tax collection order was issued. The amount was not large, totaling about 2 million yuan. The bank first paid a 2.5% export tax, and then paid an additional 7.5% and 5.25% new tax, totaling more than 170,000 yuan for the new tax, combined with the already paid 2.5% tax, totaling more than 200,000 yuan. After the customs collected this tax rate, it was allowed to ship the bank's silver to the United States. This is the first batch shipped out of Shanghai after the silver tax collection balance tax and the first huge tax revenue income of the Jianghai Customs since the issuance of the silver tax collection.

Lifting the Ban on Rice and Grain in Shashi 149

Telegraph Urges Shanghai to Send Ships for Loading

The Shashi authorities, yielding to telegram requests from the local Chamber of Commerce and various sectors, have lifted the ban on exporting rice. This has been approved, and starting from October 21st, rice can be loaded and shipped out. Rice merchants from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Anhui have been notified and are rushing to Shashi for procurement and transport. A large quantity has already been purchased and finalized, awaiting loading onto ships. Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received urgent telegrams from Shashi, roughly stating: After the ban on rice exports was lifted, there is a significant amount of rice awaiting transport in Shashi. Foreign merchant ships are already competing to secure loading contracts. The telegrams requested that Chinese merchant shipping companies in Shanghai quickly dispatch a large number of iron barges and 1,000-ton, shallow-draft river steamers to Shashi to transport large quantities of rice to Shanghai. Currently, companies such as China Merchants and Sanbei are preparing to send ships for loading. However, as Shashi is located upstream on the Yangtze River during the low-water season, the water level is minimal in the section between Chenglingji and Jianli, making navigation difficult. For example, the heavily loaded Yongsheng vessel of the Yongan Company ran aground near Jianli and is currently being lightened and towed to safety. The Yongsheng vessel has a deeper draft and is not suitable for navigating the middle section of the Yangtze River. It is common for unregulated ships to be stranded upstream during the dry season. According to the company, the hull of the ship is undamaged. According to shipping industry sources, the first batch of Shashi rice is expected to arrive in Shanghai by the end of this month.

Anhui Rice Export Ban Lifted 150

Imposing a 5% Disaster Relief Donation

Purchasing from Outside the Province Is No Longer Economical

Anhui Province, due to the severe drought this year, had previously restricted the export of rice and grain to maintain local food security. However, the central government believes that food regulation is a matter of national importance and did not allow the ban to continue. Therefore, the ban was lifted on the 15th of this month. However, to provide relief to disaster victims, a levy of five sheng per shi (equivalent to 5%) is collected on grain transported to other provinces, to be used for disaster relief. Since this regulation was implemented, the price is no longer competitive. Procurement from other areas is no longer profitable because the cost is similar to the selling price. As a result, no Anhui rice has been shipped to Shanghai so far.

Ministry of Industry Sends Officials to Shanghai 151

To Investigate the Current Status of Grain Production and Sales

According to the Central News Agency, grain merchants in Shanghai previously reported that the fluctuating prices of grain were causing instability not only for businesses but also for farmers and the entire populace. They requested assistance from the Ministry of Industry. The Ministry of Industry has dispatched officials to Shanghai to investigate the price fluctuations of various grains over the past year, as well as the current state of production and sales. Once the investigation is completed, the Ministry will issue instructions to determine relief measures.
