Two Important Letters from the Municipal Federation 155

Opposing the Municipal Council's Increase in Hotel Taxes

Requesting a Ban on Impersonating Soldiers and Selling Goods Along the Way

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation sent letters yesterday to the Public Concession Municipal Council, opposing the increase in hotel taxes, and submitted a petition to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, requesting a ban on impersonating soldiers and selling goods along the way. The two letters are excerpted as follows:

Opposing the Increase in Hotel Taxes 156

Esteemed Sirs, we have received a letter from the Shanghai Hotel Association requesting that we negotiate with the Municipal Council to abolish the increase in property taxes. We agree. Property tax collection should be based on property deeds and should not be arbitrarily increased or disrupt tax collection. There is no reason for this. There have been countless instances of such inflated tax assessments. If your council wishes to increase revenue, it should collect taxes on vacant properties to lower property prices and attract residents, thereby maintaining the market and increasing revenue. Furthermore, it is hoped that you will economize internally, reduce the number of highly paid Westerners, and employ diligent Chinese people in their positions, which would help maintain the budget. This should not be limited to the hotel industry. We respectfully submit this letter for your consideration. Respectfully, to the General Manager of the Public Concession Municipal Council.

Requesting a Ban on Soldiers Selling Goods 157

Petitioning for the investigation and banning of individuals impersonating soldiers and forcibly selling goods along the way. We request that your esteemed headquarters strictly prohibit this to uphold military discipline and national dignity. Our member shops have reported to the association, and the association has sent representatives to investigate. Recently, along the roads of the Chinese Concession, individuals resembling soldiers have been forcibly soliciting and selling goods, with fierce expressions and terrifying appearances, disturbing both Chinese and foreigners. Such behavior damages military prestige and violates military discipline, affecting the reputation of our country's military and disrupting travelers. If this is not strictly prohibited, it will seriously affect national dignity and public image. We respectfully submit this petition to your esteemed headquarters, requesting that you order a strict prohibition to maintain military discipline and uphold national law, for the public good. Respectfully submitted.

The Municipal Industrial Society Plans to Build a Water Plant in Pudong 158

The Pudong area of Shanghai is vast, with numerous factories. The completion of Pudong Avenue has led to an increasing population density. To date, there is no tap water facility, which is crucial for drinking water hygiene and fire prevention. Mayor Wu, recognizing the importance of this, believes that there is a need for active planning. Yesterday, he instructed the Secretariat to send a letter to the Municipal Industrial Trust Society to actively plan for this. The Society, upon receiving the letter from the Municipal Government Secretariat, adhering to the Municipal Government's consistent vision of promoting the prosperity of the city and Mayor Wu's concern for the welfare of the people of Pudong, has already begun preparations.

Newspaper Reports Tripartite Understanding Reached on Cross-Border Road Construction Zone 159

Hope for Signature After Feisinger Returns to Shanghai

According to the Japanese newspaper "Mainichi Shimbun," an understanding has been reached between the Chinese side, the Municipal Council, and the Japanese side regarding the establishment of a special zone for cross-border road construction. However, disagreements remain on the details. Because Municipal Council Director-General Feisinger is currently on leave in his home country, negotiations have stalled. On the other hand, the interests of our nationals (Japanese) are significant. This time, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs dispatched Mr. Sone of the East Asia Bureau to Shanghai to investigate the actual situation. He left Shanghai on the 17th. Consul Sugihara, head of the Consulate-General, has also held discussions on this issue. He will report to Beijing soon. The main points of the negotiation progress are investigated as follows: (1) The issue of the police organization within the special zone; (2) The issue of the scope of the special zone; (3) The issue of public utilities in the special zone. Regarding the issue of the organization of the special police, it is stipulated that in the northern and western special zones, the director-general will be Chinese, the deputy director-general will be Western, and the candidate for director-general will be Japanese. Next is the issue of the scope of the second special zone. There are also clear regulations regarding security and other relationships. However, various difficulties have arisen in practice regarding the method of road demarcation. For example, opinions were presented to the Chinese side on whether to expand or change the scope in a certain area, or to reduce it in another place, and specific plans were discussed. As for the third issue of public utilities, clear regulations have also been made regarding issues such as gas, telephones, water, and fire protection, in order to reach an agreement. All the general outlines have been decided. Once Municipal Council Director-General Feisinger returns to Shanghai, the formal signature can take place.

Special Survey Record of National Goods Industry 161

(8) Bakelite Industry

Bakelite is a newly emerging industry. The first company to be established was the Yaguang Bakelite Factory, founded by Mr. Zhang Huikang. Initially, it only produced daily necessities, such as rice bowls, spoons, basins, and plates. First, it was bakelite, and then it created bakelite jade. Its products were novel, beautiful, and durable, and were well-received by the public. As a result, sales were wide and profits were high. Many businessmen envied its low capital and high profits, and established factories to imitate it. Currently, there are more than ten such factories, not including small factories. As the number of factories increased, competition became fierce, and they competed by lowering prices, even below cost. Therefore, factories such as Yaguang, Shanghai Jiao Mu, and Shanghai Industrial initiated the organization of a trade association. Nine companies joined the trade association. The reporter specially interviewed Mr. Zhang Huikang, manager of Yaguang Bakelite Factory, a leader in the industry. The information obtained from the conversation is briefly recorded as follows: The bakelite jade industry is a newly emerging industry with a history of only four years. Last year's sales were about 500,000 yuan. The products of Yaguang Manufacturing Factory were well received by all parties, so its sales accounted for about half of the total. Chinese people are imitative and lack creativity. Whenever they see a newly emerging industry, regardless of its high or low cost, or wide or narrow sales, they flock to it. The bakelite jade industry also suffers from the same problem. This year, another five or six new companies have opened. They are small in scale and have little capital. They produce crude and shoddy products and operate independently, resulting in chaotic market prices and increasingly fierce competition. The trade association was established on the sixth floor of the Continental Commercial Center. Nine companies joined. The larger companies can still unite, gradually revise commissions, discounts, etc., and the market price is gradually becoming consistent. However, the seven or eight companies that have not joined continue to compete by lowering prices and secretly offering discounts, greatly affecting the business of other factories. Recently, considering the chaotic market prices and the inability of the association to control them, each factory has launched a secondary brand to reduce costs and engage in mass production to compete with other factories. This effort is extremely laborious. The raw materials for bakelite jade are mostly imported from countries such as Germany and the United States. After more than two years of painstaking research, Yaguang Factory is now able to produce its own bakelite raw materials. From now on, the main raw materials will no longer need to be imported from abroad. This can be said to be a good sign for the domestic goods industry. The production of bakelite jade products is relatively simple. However, the mold manufacturing must be accurate and precise, and the mold design must be novel and ingenious. Although bakelite jade work is easy, it is difficult to ensure excellent quality. The upper and lower temperature, the high and low pressure, and the long and short time can all affect the quality. The inferior products on the market, although similar in appearance to the products of superior factories such as Yaguang, are not durable. This is because they cut corners and reduce materials. All aspects of temperature, pressure, time, and composition are without standards. Therefore, inferior goods on the market lose their luster after only a few days of use, and emit an odor when exposed to water, which is a reef hindering the future of promoting domestic goods. Although the bakelite jade industry's products this year seem to be improving day by day, sales have not kept pace. This is because rural areas have gone bankrupt in recent years, and the purchasing power of the public is extremely weak. In addition, competition among colleagues, frequent discounts, and falling prices make the future of production and sales uncertain. Statistics show that among the colleagues, two have closed down within a few months of opening, and several are on the verge of collapse. Most of them overestimate their abilities and covet high profits, leading to a complete failure and no chance of recovery. In this precarious situation, there will naturally be many eliminated within the year. Upon investigation, most of the emerging colleagues are established by general craftsmen who arouse the curiosity of investors. The capital is small and the skills are limited, and the products are limited to simple items such as plates and bowls. These products are already being abandoned by large factories, and they all embrace the principle of small profits and dumping. Small factories suffer a major blow from the beginning, and lack the ability to open up new avenues. They have to sit and wait for death. This is the biggest reason for failure. Currently, the trend in this industry is that large colleagues are actively promoting the scope of application of bakelite jade, and the manufacturing methods are becoming more sophisticated. Small colleagues take on the production of small parts for others, and rely on others to make wedding dresses. Of course, they can only sigh with admiration. However, there is one thing that is gratifying: bakelite jade daily necessities can already replace foreign goods. However, a large number of foreign electrical products are still imported. This industry should actively improve equipment, simplify work, reduce consumption, and promote sales. Then the goal of excluding foreign goods can be achieved. Yaguang's products are becoming more and more refined, so this year's business is not much different from last year. The person in charge is an electrical engineering expert, and the future goal is the manufacture of electrical appliances and motors. Now it has increased its capital to 250,000 yuan and is already preparing for the manufacture of electrical appliances. It will then manufacture motors, which will make a great contribution to our country's ongoing construction. Visiting the entire factory work, the accuracy is accurate and meticulous, and the machine equipment is particularly exquisite, purely in line with scientific management methods, which is truly commendable in the bakelite jade industry.

Wang Dizhong and Others Set Sail Yesterday Morning 163

The Postal Savings Bureau Sent Representatives to See Them Off

They Will Be Able to Return Home in the Spring of the Year After Next

Wang Dizhong, Zhang Qigong, Wang Yie, Wang Zishuang, Lu Jiajun, and other six specialists sent by the Ministry of Communications to Austria to study postal savings, completed their departure procedures and set sail yesterday morning on the German postal ship "Columbus". The ship was anchored at 8:00 AM yesterday. The Postal Savings Bureau of this port also sent representatives to the dock to see them off. According to specialist Wang Dizhong's words to the reporter of the "Nichi Nichi" (Everyday News) newspaper on the verge of leaving, after our group of six arrives in Austria, we will first contact the Austrian Postal Savings Bureau to negotiate study methods. The study period in Austria is scheduled for one and a half years, one year for research and half a year for practical work. We will return to China in the spring of the year after next (25). The results of the Austrian Research Institute will be reported to the Ministry for adoption at any time.

The Magistrate of Deqing County Comes to Shanghai to Beg for Relief 165

The People Live on Tofu Dregs and Bran

Deqing County in Zhejiang Province is located in the west of Zhejiang Province, under the jurisdiction of the old Huzhou Prefecture, bordering the four counties of Wuxing, Wukang, Hangzhou, and Chongde. It has always been a silkworm-raising area. In recent years, the silk cocoon harvest has been terrible, and the people have been living in poverty. Nine out of ten families are empty. This is not just a matter of today or tomorrow. This year, there was no rain during the rainy season. From mid-May to the end of August, there was no rain for a total of ninety-eight days. The soil and rocks were scorched, the early rice withered, and most of the late rice could not be planted. The total farmland in the county is 376,700 mu, of which about 75,000 mu had no harvest, about 187,000 mu were seriously affected, and about 114,000 mu had some hope of harvest. The total population of the county is 178,300, of which more than 90,000 are affected by the disaster. The disaster is so great that it is unprecedented in the past hundred years. Currently, the affected farmers live on tofu dregs and bran. Chen Huan, the magistrate of the county, has come to Shanghai to appeal to save the people. Yesterday, Chen County Magistrate was accompanied by Yu Saicheng, Yuan Songfan, Yu Zhongxian, Mo Jilin, and other gentlemen from Shanghai who are natives of the county, to the Chinese and foreign relief associations, the drought relief associations of various provinces, the All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association, the Lake District Disaster Relief Association, the Red Swastika Society, the Red Cross Society, and other charitable organizations to beg for relief. Each association expressed sympathy and promised to find ways to provide relief.

Song and Han Navigation United Petitioning Delegation's Petition 166

The Song and Han Navigation United Petitioning Delegation, because the Shanghai Navigation Management Committee ordered the cancellation of the Song and Han Navigation qualification, starting from October 1st, and not allowing service, specially submitted a petition to the central government and various ministries to fight for it yesterday. The original petition stated that it was to use false names, plunder real power, exterminate the inherent powers of the Chinese people, expand the power of foreigners, conspiracies, and harm the country and the people. We urge a thorough investigation and swift prevention. The profession of navigation is related to national defense and military secrets. In all countries in the world, there is almost no example of allowing foreigners to serve as navigators within their territory. Our country, because the Qing Dynasty authorities did not understand maritime affairs and abandoned sovereignty, the navigation of each port was occupied by foreigners, which became a common practice. Currently, the only remaining piece of fruit that can maintain the remnant situation is the Yangtze River line. My colleagues have been practicing here for a long time, like the pioneers. However, over the years, foreigners have been deliberately trying to exclude the Chinese people from the Yangtze River navigation in order to fulfill their extravagant hope of complete monopoly. Threats and inducements have already been used to the extreme. My colleagues have always adhered to the principle of dying rather than letting go. The oppression we have suffered is deeply painful and cannot be fully described. Last year, the government established the Navigation Management Committee in accordance with the purpose of recovering navigation sovereignty. However, the power in the committee is controlled by the maritime customs commissioners, who, in the name of the Shanghai Navigation Management Committee, canceled our qualifications with illegal orders, and did not allow us to serve as before from October 1st. Arbitrary manipulation is nothing more than creating monopoly opportunities for foreigners. This is presented separately to your departments and offices: (1) Chinese Yangtze River navigation has been the earliest profession in history, and the territorial sovereignty belongs to our country. My colleagues not only studied and graduated from the Navigation Training Institute sponsored by the Navy Department and obtained certificates, navigation licenses, and other documents, allowing them to serve, but also each person has been engaged in practical navigation for at least five or six years, and up to one or twenty years. Whether in terms of laws or achievements, there is no reason why they cannot serve as navigators. According to the example, navigation is a public business, similar to the practice of law, and is subject to national restrictions. In addition, within the approved area, they can operate freely. This situation is just like my colleagues graduating from school and passing the examination, all legal qualifications, serving as Yangtze River navigators, is the approved service area. May I ask, what power does the maritime customs commissioner have to prohibit it? (2) The navigation examination law promulgated by the Examination Yuan, its examination power is controlled by the Examination Yuan. Before Rong Qing held the examination, we did not hear of it being approved, and we did not see it being announced after the event, making it impossible to understand its content. My colleagues also went to participate in this examination to explore its inside story. (Omission) Things are like a child's play. The reason for this is that there are other intentions. However, we, in the relationship with our colleagues, are not willing to expose more about the utilization of the Chinese people. One example can be used to infer the rest. (3) Navigators have the right to operate freely. Whether long-term navigation or short-term navigation, the income is not subject to any exploitation. The previous Song and Han Navigation Association was opposed by our people because of the collection of dividends. Now, the maritime customs commissioner is actually intensifying the situation and depriving our colleagues of the right to operate freely. The compensation method they have set is to completely own the income of each person. In the collection of navigation fees, after removing the expenses of the Shanghai Navigation Management Committee, if there is a surplus, a little bit of profit can be shared. The public principle is changed to a monopoly, and you can sit on the ground and divide the spoils without any cost. There is nothing more than this for the so-called business without capital. Furthermore, I heard that the maritime customs commissioner's plan is on the one hand to raise several foreigners so that they have food to eat, and on the other hand to hope for a surplus to offset a certain appropriation. His intention is biased, nothing is more than this. (4) Yangtze River navigation is not monopolized by the Chinese people. There are still foreign navigators of British, German, and Japanese nationality who are in control. If the maritime customs commissioner has no other intentions and focuses on recovering our country's sovereignty, then foreign navigators should be banned first. They cannot be allowed to continue to serve. They reverse the priorities, oppose Chinese navigators, add various restrictions, and create this bad example. Their conspiracies and schemes are like snakes and scorpions. Chinese navigators have a fixed number, which is under their jurisdiction. Why is the foreign part completely let go and allowed to be free? As for the Chinese navigation fee, it is lower than that of foreigners, which is a way to attract foreign business. Now it is deliberately increased. It is clearly to drive away the birds from the bushes, and on the contrary, it is praised as raising the treatment of navigation. The deceiving words can be said to be the heart of Sima Zhao, which is known to everyone. (5) The Chinese people's service as Yangtze River navigators is not obtained by luck. If they are so devastated by the commissioner, it means that the occupations of dozens of our colleagues will be abandoned, which is not a lifelong abandonment, the extinction of life, and the relatives who are waiting to die, what about hundreds of people? Is this kind of evil and absurd act inflicted on the Chinese people? May I ask, is it still bearable in law or in emotion? Now that my colleagues have been placed in a dead end by foreigners, they have no choice but to fight to the death. My colleagues are based on illegal and unfair reasons. One is that it is greatly contrary to our country's purpose of recovering navigation. Secondly, the examination power is related to our country's internal affairs. How can foreigners overstep the bounds and make plans for us? Moreover, in Yangtze River navigation, there are still the positions occupied by British, German, and Japanese foreigners. Why does the maritime customs commissioner not ban them and only target our Chinese people? He examines under the false name of the committee, arbitrarily dismisses them. If he does not correct them immediately, then in the future, the maritime customs commissioner will use the false name of recovering navigation to plunder real power. Unless the Chinese navigation is completely ruined. In short, foreigners have a hundred and one tricks to exclude the Chinese people, to protect their own kind, and to be as poisonous as snakes and vipers. My colleagues have been oppressed by this, and they have to fight absolutely and consistently. For this reason, we have listed the facts and respectfully ask your departments and offices to review and approve them, and to swiftly order the maritime customs to abolish the previous selection and restore the old navigation personnel to serve together, in order to protect sovereignty and maintain the whole. This presentation is to the National Government, the General Staff Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Navy, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Communications, presented by the Song and Han Navigation United Petitioning Delegation.

Preliminary Rectification of Coal Prices in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 169

Coal Barge Industry Association Requests Assistance from the Chamber of Commerce

The Coal Barge Industry Association of this city sent a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that according to reports from member boat companies in the north and south of the city, coal freight rates in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have been chaotic recently. Some coal merchants have even demanded that boat owners reduce freight rates, otherwise they will refuse to load coal. If unforeseen circumstances occur en route, boat owners will be required to compensate, placing boat merchants in a situation of utter ruin. They requested prompt relief. Upon receiving the letter, it was submitted to the joint meeting of the 13th session of the second council of executive and supervisory committee members for discussion. It was generally agreed that the association's coal freight rate list for Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces was formulated based on social living conditions and cost accounting and had been submitted to and approved by the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau for implementation. All members of the industry in the city were notified to comply in order to safeguard their business. The association had previously sent a letter to your esteemed chamber, requesting that you forward it to the Coal Industry Association of this city, notifying all coal companies, which is on record. Given the aforementioned situation, the chaotic freight rates are a matter of concern for the entire boat industry. After deliberation, it was decided that if coal merchants hire boats to load coal without adhering to the association's freight rate list, boat owners will not be responsible for any unforeseen circumstances that may occur en route. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce is requested to send another letter to the Coal Industry Association, notifying all coal merchants for their information, which is on record. Accordingly, this letter is sent for your review and prompt approval and forwarding in order to maintain commercial transportation, etc.

Rickshaw Merchants in the Special District Held an Emergency Meeting of Representatives Yesterday 170

Considerations Regarding the New Rickshaw Sample of the Public Works Department Have Been Found to Contradict the Agreement

Expressed Opposition to Arbitrarily Replacing Existing Old Vehicles

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Rickshaw Industry Association of this city's Special District held an emergency meeting of member representatives at its headquarters on Lloyd Road at 3 p.m. yesterday because the Public Works Department changed the rickshaw sample and rejected the rickshaw merchants' suggestions. More than 90 people attended, with Gu Songmao, Yin Zhiling, and Hou Shao'an serving as the presidium. The results of the discussion were as follows: (1) The new rickshaw sample formulated by the Public Works Department was not agreed upon by the rickshaw merchants and violated the agreement of equal consultation on August 6. Therefore, all members unanimously decided to use the new sample designated by Gu Songmao as the standard. (2) If permission cannot be obtained from the Public Works Department, the association will invite rickshaw merchants to petition the Public Works Department again. (3) Opposition to the Public Works Department arbitrarily replacing existing old vehicles. (4) Investigate the existing old-style new vehicles. After the investigation, a list will be submitted to the Public Works Department requesting general use to be used up, in order to avoid losses.

The Case of Embezzlement by the Accountant of the China Coal Ball Company Awaits Further Summons 171

Wu Zhensheng, an accountant from Shaoxing employed by the China Coal Ball Company at 26 Dixiwei Road, had been working for the company for five years. He resigned last winter. In March of this year, a shareholders' meeting revealed that he had embezzled silver taels 3,000 and yuan 8,499.16 between September 23, 1930, and January 27 of last year. Yang Zhuang, a Ningbo woman and shareholder, reported the case to the Hongkou Police Station. Detectives were dispatched to arrest Wu and bring him to the First Special District Court. Wu testified that the money had been used by the deceased major shareholder, Li Futang, a Ningbo native. Li Yao, Li Futang's wife, appeared in court and admitted that she would be responsible for it. However, the shareholders stated that there were still discrepancies in the accounts handled by the defendant. Wu was ordered to pay a deposit of 10,000 yuan and released pending further investigation after the accounts were clarified. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zeshan presided over a continued hearing in the third criminal court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, recounted the events, stating that the case needed to be adjourned because the truth of the accounts could not be determined immediately. Jiang Baoli, a lawyer representing the plaintiff, stated that Li Futang, a shareholder, had established the Houde Coal Company at the time and transferred more than 50,000 yuan from the China Coal Ball Company for his own use. When questioned about whether the defendant had appeared on time after being released, Fan Gang, the defendant's lawyer, stated that the accountant hired by the plaintiff had a family relationship with the plaintiff and was likely biased and unable to handle the matter impartially. Therefore, the client also wanted to hire an accountant to allow both parties to calculate the accounts in detail and hope for fairness, etc. Judge Wu ordered the defendant to pay the original deposit and adjourned the hearing to the afternoon of the 30th for further verification.

Three Cases Occurred at the Intersection of Zhongxing Road and Datong Road in Zhabei 173

Crushed to Death... Died on the Road... Suicide by Poison

At the intersection of Zhongxing Road and Datong Road in Zhabei, at approximately 7 p.m. the night before last, a No. 9545 coal truck traveling from west to east was delivering coal to the Qianyi Glass Factory. Unexpectedly, while passing the entrance of Chengren Lane, it was unable to avoid a young boy, who was knocked down and had his head crushed by the wheels, resulting in immediate death. Officer Shi Ze'en of Post No. 42 learned of the incident and immediately sent the driver responsible for the accident, along with the coal truck, to the Taiyang Temple Police Station for transfer to the Xinzha Public Security Bureau. At the same time, guarantor Wang Shaoting reported the case to the Shanghai Local Court yesterday for examination. At approximately 4 p.m., Prosecutor Ouyang Shu arrived to examine the body and determined that the deceased, Chen Changlin, 14 years old, had been crushed to death before his death. It was also learned that the deceased was an apprentice at the Qianyi Glass Factory and that his father, Chen Liangwei, had six children and lived at No. 1 Jvde Lane, Taiyang Temple Road, where he made a living pulling a rickshaw. Also, at approximately 3 p.m. yesterday, at the corner of Datong Road (opposite the second team of the Pengpu Security Corps), a man resembling a beggar, approximately 30 years old, suddenly collapsed and died. He was wearing a blue cloth jacket and pants, had a shaved head, and wore white socks without shoes. The body was examined at the same time, and no family members were found. The guarantor was instructed to arrange for burial. In addition, Lin Yutian, 34 years old, a Ningbo native who jointly opened a carpentry shop making tennis rackets at No. 11 Chengren Lane, suddenly took poison at approximately 8 a.m. yesterday. His partners, Xu Bingzhang and Zhou Jiashui, sent him to the Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road. A medicine bottle was found next to his pillow. After examination by the doctor, it was determined that the medicine was Cola medicine. His life is in danger and he is currently unable to speak. His partners, Xu Bingzhang and Zhou Jiashui, have been sent to the Xinzha Public Security Bureau. It is said that he owed Hengfeng Wood Company on Tiantong Road 100 yuan for goods and was unable to pay on time, leading to this.

The Case of Pan Wenxia Being Accused: Does the Film Company Have a Role to Play? 174

Pan Wenxia, the lead actress in the Meihua Film Company's sound film "Song of the Rose," signed a contract with the company on August 1 of this year for a period of 12 months, with a stipulated monthly salary of 70 yuan. The contract also stipulated that after signing, Pan must be under the company's direction. Because Pan was born on the sixth day of the tenth lunar month of the third year of the Republic of China, although she is nominally 21 years old, she is actually not yet 20 years old. Therefore, her father, Pan Qiqing, also signed the contract as her legal representative. Recently, when Pan went to the Shanghai Film Company on the 28th of last month to shoot a fashion film, Meihua Company prevented her from doing so. As a result, Lawyer Tang Hao filed a complaint with the criminal division of the First Special District Court, accusing Pan of violating Article 366 of the Criminal Law for breach of trust. After a preliminary hearing, the case was adjourned because Pan's address was incorrect and she could not be summoned. These details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yuzhu opened the first criminal court for a summons. Pan did not appear again. Judge Liu announced that the bailiff had reported that when attempting to summon Pan, the person at 107 Lane 460, Aivanyi Road, stated that Pan had moved. Therefore, the summons was returned. Zhu Ruifeng was then summoned to the court. According to his testimony, the company's working hours were from 8 a.m. to 6 p.m., and the defendant went to the Shanghai Company to film without the company's permission on the 28th, which was indeed a breach of trust, etc. Zhou Yinong, the manager of the Yunrong Company, testified that on the 25th of last month, the company held a fashion show at the Vienna Ballroom and invited Pan Wenxia to participate. Zhu Ruifeng had approved this. At that time, the Shanghai Company was filming news footage on the spot, and Zhu also witnessed it. Later, because several shots needed to be reshot, Pan was invited to the Shanghai Company to reshoot on the 28th. Zhu was consulted beforehand, and Zhu said that as long as Pan agreed, there was no problem. Moreover, after this lawsuit, Pan continued to film at Meihua every day. According to rumors, this lawsuit actually had a purpose, etc. However, Zhu denied that there was any purpose and stated that he had never allowed her to film at the Shanghai Company, etc. Judge Liu then ordered the case to be adjourned for one week for further hearing. If Pan does not appear again, a warrant will be issued for her arrest. The court was then adjourned.

The China National Road Construction Association Held a Membership Solicitation Meeting Yesterday 175

More Than 300 People Attended, Including Kong Xiangxi and Wang Zhengting

The China National Road Construction Association held its 14th anniversary membership solicitation meeting at the New Asia Hotel on the 7th floor yesterday afternoon, starting at 6 p.m. More than 300 people attended, including team leaders and guests. President Wang specially sent Chu Minyi to Shanghai to participate. The details are as follows:

Attendees 176

President Wang (represented by Chu Minyi), Mao Yun representing the Municipal Party Department, General Captain Kong Xiangxi, Chief of Staff Chu Minyi, Commander-in-Chief Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Yu Zuoting representing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Chairman Wang Zhengting, Secretary-General Fan Zhenchu, Committee Members Xu Shiying, Zhao Jinqing, Wu Kaisheng, Cao Yunxiang, Zhu Shaoping, Qu Yingguang, Yang Nianzu, Hu Guigeng, Li Zhaohuan, Chen Guangfu, Huang Jingwan, Wang Dasui, Yang Xiaotian, Shen Hegao, Zhao Shouyu, Lu Ganchen, Xie Chengyu, Shen Junru, Liu Yunfang, Liu Wendao, Zhang Ming, Weng Zhilong, Wang Kunxi, Cai Xiaobai, and more than 300 team leaders and members.

1. Dinner, 2. Meeting, 3. Formalities, 4. Reading of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Will, 5. Chairman's welcome speech and report on the main points of the meeting, 6. Secretary-General's report on the overview of membership solicitation, 7. Speeches by the General Captain, Commander-in-Chief, and Chief of Staff, 8. Speeches by Party and government representatives, 9. Speeches by team leaders and guests, 10. Photography,

Chairman's Speech 178

Chairman Wang Zhengting said in his speech, briefly, that he was honored to have everyone participate in today's 14th membership solicitation meeting. He felt that there were many participants today, which could also show our cooperative efforts. Transportation is the most important work to help national construction, and road construction is especially important in transportation construction. Therefore, the National Road Construction Association was established to awaken the people of the country to the awareness of road construction. At the beginning of the establishment of the Road Construction Association, the national highway was only 1,000 kilometers. Until recently, the highway construction in various provinces has expanded to 97,000 kilometers, which shows the necessity of road construction and publicity. Secondly, how to continue to promote and maintain roads and protect roads is the most important cause and responsibility to be carried out in the second step. The function of building roads is not only convenient for bandit prevention and military affairs, but also has great economic benefits. For example, Jiangxi recently has made great progress in road construction, and the Red Bandits have therefore been unable to use their tactics. In short, as long as we have more comrades, things will be easier to develop and succeed, etc.

Kong Xiangxi's Speech 179

The Prime Minister once resigned from the task of being the President and took over the task of being the National Railway Superintendent, which shows the importance that the late Prime Minister attached to road construction. When I was in Shanxi Province a few years ago, I deeply felt the inconvenience of transportation in Shanxi and the difficulties of the people's travel and the great economic losses. Therefore, I suggested to Chairman Yan Baichuan to build roads. Chairman Yan also felt the importance of road construction, so he began to order the armory to build roads to facilitate the people's travel. Later, when I arrived in Shanghai, I and Mr. Wang Rutang and others jointly organized the National Road Association to promote the road building movement. Now the national roads have gradually been built. What is needed now is how to maintain the roads and improve the roads. What is especially important is the source of cars and gasoline. Because if we have highways, but lack cars and gasoline, it is still not complete. Therefore, we should pay attention to how we build cars and supply our own car fuel to recover our rights. Therefore, in order to achieve the above-mentioned goals, on the one hand, we must actively let the general public know the importance of building roads, and at the same time, we must actively cultivate specialized talents to solve the fundamental problems of developing China's transportation. This is the whole meaning of promoting road construction, etc.

Chu Minyi's Speech 180

Chu Minyi, representative of President Wang, gave a speech saying that everyone knows that to revitalize national construction, transportation construction is a particularly important task. Therefore, I believe that to build China, we must start with building transportation. Therefore, the establishment and work of the China National Road Construction Association has great significance. Regarding the issue of transportation tools after the highway is built, I believe that when China cannot manufacture cars and does not have gasoline, promoting horse-drawn carriages is the only way to make up for it. Because in the inland countryside, horse-drawn carriages are indeed a more suitable means of transportation. However, promoting horse-drawn carriages is not regressing, because it is like we usually eat shark fin and sea cucumber. When necessary, we will eat some green vegetables and tofu. I hope everyone understands this point. Promoting horse-drawn carriages does have many advantages in China, etc.

Liu Wendao's Speech 182

Then, Liu Wendao, our country's ambassador to Italy, gave a speech, saying that he had three thoughts on this visit: (1) Roads are related to enriching the country in peacetime, (2) Roads are related to military affairs in wartime, and (3) Roads can nationalize the country and unify the country's culture. The development of cause must start with transportation. When I was in Germany, I saw that the country's causes were developed all near the Rhine, and I felt the importance of transportation. With the development of transportation, the number of cars will inevitably increase. Therefore, car factories will naturally produce in large quantities. Now, because of the progress of science, car machines are unified and simplified, and parts can be used in other industries. Therefore, the first conclusion is that although enriching the country does not rely on road construction, the development of road administration can help enrich the country. Second, after a country's national crisis, in addition to the renewal of railways, it also demarcated several provinces to build car roads, so that every three hours there can be a car passing through, winning our country with a certain time. Once something happens, we must seek to concentrate our military strength. Therefore, in addition to strengthening the army, we must first build roads. Therefore, the second conclusion is that although strengthening the army does not necessarily require road construction, there is no doubt that road construction can help strengthen the army. Third, I just returned from abroad, and I was so stimulated that I always remembered the national crisis. I often thought of the New Life Movement. The New Life Movement is to be orderly, to be proper and orderly, and to be clean and honest is to be orderly. Otherwise, there is no order. The roads in Berlin and Rome are very clean from morning to night, and the sidewalks on the left and right are orderly. In our country, it is a mess. This is the result of the lack of order and discipline in the hearts of the people. You can see from the small that the degree of civilization of a country can be seen from the way you walk. Maintaining a neat and solemn form in peacetime will cultivate a firm and unyielding will. The social people have a spirit of the rule of law, and then they can help each other and support the leaders, and go to the national crisis together under a leader. The chairman, the commander-in-chief, and others have worked hard to promote road construction for 14 years, which is of great relationship with the national revival. Because of the neat roads, the habit of observing discipline is cultivated, assisting the central government, and organizing a vigorous movement to avenge the shame. After that, Mr. Liu's speech was passionate and generous, and the audience was moved. Then Mr. Wang Zhengting gave a closing speech, and each person was given a copy of the Road Monthly, and they dispersed happily.

The Wages of the Zhonghua Iron Factory Were All Robbed 186

A Loss of 1,700 Yuan

And the Workers' Clothes Were Robbed

Wang Zuocai, 32 years old, a native of Songjiang, the manager of the Zhonghua Iron Factory at No. 30, Lujiabang Road, Nanshi, the factory employs more than 100 workers. Yesterday was the day when the factory paid the wages to the workers, so he withdrew 1,700 yuan of banknotes from the Bank of China. The wages were about to be distributed to the workers by name in the accounting room. At 3:30 p.m. yesterday, four robbers suddenly came. One of the robbers was wearing a black vest and a copper basin felt hat. The others were wearing blue cloth shirts and trousers. The robbers spoke the Jiangbei dialect and the local dialect. The robbers divided into one robber to guard the door and the rest broke into the factory, shouting and forbidding any noise, first cutting off the telephone line, and then supervising many partners in the factory in one place, and robbing all the 1,700 yuan of banknotes for paying wages in the accounting room, and also searching and robbing the clothes of the partners in the factory. The robbers gained the stolen goods and fled to the north. Wang Zuocai, the manager of the factory, ordered Zhang Yongkang, the general affairs officer of the factory, to report to the Ximen Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and ask them to order the arrest. Director Li of the branch believed that the case involved the robbery of factory wages and was a major case, so he immediately dispatched detectives to strictly arrest them.

The Trial of the Doctor Accused of Illegally Manufacturing Morphine Opens 187

Qian Baiyan Denies Involvement in Manufacturing

Workers Testify That It Was Made into Medicated Water

Qian Baiyan, also known as Qian Mian, a native of Zhenjiang, 25 years old, who lives at No. 4, Yinyu Lane, Mai Gao Baolu Road, French Concession, opened a Xinsheng Hospital in the shop downstairs at No. 799-801, Aiduya Road. Recently, due to the economic downturn, the two or three floors of the building were vacant and no one rented them. Therefore, he and Zhang Sen, a Ningbo native who lived at No. 25, Hengye Lane, No. 1414, Aiduya Road, jointly invested in setting up an illegal morphine manufacturing organization in the Xinsheng Hospital, secretly manufacturing and selling it, and making a lot of profit. Unexpectedly, the matter was not secret. Recently, Guo Bole, the West Inspector of the French Police, found out and led Inspector Li Yaolong, Detective Zhang Daorong, Bao Detective Liu Jinrong, Shen Jinshu, and others to search the organization at 9 a.m. on the 5th of this month. They arrested the boss Qian Baiyan and seven other accomplices, including Lu Xianglong, Li Asan, Yang Xin, Zhang Jinfu, Zhu Huaming, and Zhang Ziwei. They seized a lot of machines and equipment and took them to the police station. However, the shareholder Zhang Sen had already heard the news and escaped without being caught. The police station had sent the defendants to the Second Special Court for trial and investigation. These details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday afternoon, Criminal Court President Wang Gangxu presided over the first criminal court for interrogation. The defendants were defended by Lawyers Wang Shizong and Tang Hao. First, Police Lawyer Gu Jixi stated the case and prosecuted according to Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. When interrogated, the defendant Qian Baiyan confessed that he had rented the house to Zhang Sen, who was at large, for a monthly rent of 120 yuan, and did not know that he was manufacturing morphine. Lu Xianglong confessed that he was a partner in the hospital, earning 20 yuan a month, and only knew that medicated water was being made upstairs, and did not know that it was morphine. Li Asan confessed that he was introduced by a friend to work as a handyman for Zhang Sen, earning 15 yuan a month, and was arrested after working for 14 days. Yang Xin confessed that he made medicated water in the organization and earned 12 yuan. Zhang Jinfu confessed that he was an old steward in the hospital and did not know what was being made upstairs. Zhu Huaming confessed that he was learning medicine from Qian Baiyan and knew that medicated water was being made upstairs. Zhang Ziwei confessed that medicated water was being made upstairs, with a total of four people. The two people in the case now are Lu and Li. The boss doesn't come often, etc. After verifying the confessions in court, he ordered the start of the debate. Later, because the case still needed to be investigated, he ordered the debate to be suspended and postponed for further investigation. The defendants were transferred to the detention center.

The Wuxian Medical Association Sent a Letter Requesting the Banning of American Doctor Lan Wen 190

Letter to the Municipal Health Bureau

American doctor Lan Wen recently came to Shanghai. After the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association exposed his so-called new method of treating tuberculosis as having no scientific basis, he secretly arrived in Suzhou and resumed various forms of promotion. The Municipal Health Bureau recently received a letter from the Wuxian Medical Association requesting measures to ban Lan Wen's activities in China. The original letter is transcribed below for public information: "We previously read in the newspaper that American doctor Lan Wen was practicing a secret method for treating lung disease in Shanghai. Your Bureau Chief and the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Medical Association successively opposed it. Because the doctor had no foothold in Shanghai, he then came to Suzhou Bo Xi Hospital and continued to practice his secret treatment. On October 6th, he held an advertising-style promotion at the hospital. More than twenty members of our association attended the lecture, but gained no understanding whatsoever. We believe that Mr. Lan has not obtained a license to practice from the Ministry of Health of our country. He rashly came to Suzhou and used a secret method for treating tuberculosis that has no scientific basis, directly conducting human experiments and exaggerating his publicity to society. Our association believes that since he has neither published achievements nor has a scientifically honest attitude, he is insulting the Chinese people and despising the medical community. We feel deeply concerned and dare not fail to report this. In addition to submitting official letters to the Wuxian County Party Headquarters, the County Government, and the National Medical Association, which will be forwarded to the Ministry of Health of the Interior, we specially send this letter to your Bureau to explain the advantages and disadvantages, quickly ban him, protect the lives of the people, and maintain national dignity. This would be in the public interest."

Another Drug Manufacturing Facility Discovered Due to a Fire on Dagu Road 194

A Coal Store Located Downstairs, the Factory on the Top Floor

Workers Fled Quietly Upon Seeing the Fire

丨Large Quantities of Raw Materials for Drug Manufacturing Seized丨

Although there are many private drug manufacturing facilities in the city, it is difficult to crack down on them because the people involved maintain strict secrecy. However, their evil deeds have reached a climax, and they have recently been plagued by repeated fires, leading to their gradual self-destruction. After Cai Bicheng's factory on Avenu Edward VII was burned down, the factory on Wuding Road was also destroyed by fire a week later. Before these two cases could be concluded, the drug manufacturing facility at 124 Dagu Road continued the trend and went up in flames. As a result, the details of the situation were exposed. The building is leased from Dehe Foreign Company for 105 yuan per month. The drug manufacturing workshop was located on the top floor. To hide it from the public, a Tianchang Coal Store was opened downstairs. At around 3 PM the day before yesterday, a fire broke out in the workshop due to carelessness during drug refining. The workers, realizing that a disaster had occurred but not daring to report it, quietly fled. The Chinese constable stationed at post number 2194 discovered the fire and immediately reported it to the Chengdu Road Police Station via telephone. Detective Yang Xinzheng and Western Detective Kena Tai rushed to the scene. After the fire brigade extinguished the fire, they entered the building to investigate. They found only coal balls worth about 100 yuan in the coal store downstairs. The third floor was a pure drug manufacturing workshop, with all the equipment, furnishings, and various instruments for making drugs, similar to Cai Bicheng's factory. Since everyone in the building had fled, it was impossible to investigate who the owner of the factory was. However, there is speculation that the factory was also established by Cai. However, this cannot be confirmed at present. In addition to the arrangement of equipment and other items, the third floor also had a steam room, a sand-drying room, and the fire originated in the pavilion room. At the time, Chinese and Western detectives seized two bags of preliminary processed yellow heroin, ten small bottles of ether, six small bottles of acid, one box of soda, one foot-operated respirator, five molds, two earthenware vats filled with yellow liquid, one iron bucket of white powder, two chimneys, and other scattered instruments such as glass bottles. They compiled a list and also found two notes with the addresses 16 Qinyuan Village, Xinzha Road, and 26 Yunle Village, Avenue Edward VII. The detectives went to investigate these two locations, but found no clues. They reported back to the detective chief, who ordered the drugs to be sent to the Public Works Department for testing and notified all police stations to arrest the drug manufacturers. Yesterday morning, police lawyer Zhang Tianyin took the list of drugs and petitioned the First Special District Court to dispose of the items. After Judge Liu Yugui questioned the circumstances of the case, he ordered that the equipment and raw materials specifically used for manufacturing opium substitutes be confiscated, the coal balls be auctioned, and the proceeds be sent to the court for safekeeping.

Hungarian Artist Comes to China to Study Chinese Dramatic Arts 197

The North China Daily News reported that Hungarian artist L. Tatz has spent three and a half years specializing in the study of Chinese stage art and hopes to conduct a systematic study of the facial makeup of Chinese actors. Mr. Tatz's studio is currently at the Astor House Hotel. The walls of his room are covered with costumes of Eastern male and female actors, vividly demonstrating the intense tonal beauty of the Eastern stage. The facial makeup, costumes, stage steps, and unique sentiments of the Eastern stage are not found in European theaters. Mr. Tatz intends to transmit the beauty of color and line in this art form to the West. Mr. Tatz is not only deeply knowledgeable in the study of drama, but is also a famous portrait painter. His works have been collected by the Fanz Josef Academy. He is eager to choose Chinese people as subjects for his paintings. Mr. Tatz also intends to establish an art school in Shanghai to recruit foreigners to specialize in the study of Eastern art. He also plans to return to his country soon to exhibit the treasures he has collected in the East over the years in major European cities.

The hosts were Xie Baosheng, Cheng Jian, and Cao Shijun. The ceremony was solemn yet simple. He Yingqin gave a congratulatory speech, encouraging the newlyweds. Verdict Announced in the Case of Rubber Factory Workers Assaulting Detectives 200

Wang Diansheng and Others Sentenced to Imprisonment

On the afternoon of the 4th of this month, at around 2 PM, at the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory on Xujiahui Road in the French Concession, a dispute arose when the labor union sent people to the factory to collect membership fees. The factory reported it to the French Police, who dispatched detectives to suppress the situation. However, the labor union refused to be persuaded and started a fight, causing detectives Li Luchuan, Wu Zhonghua, and Tan Yunsheng to be beaten and injured. The police received information and dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to arrest Wang Diansheng, a Nanjing native and member of the labor union's standing committee, as well as workers Zhao Muhai, Ren Youfeng, Xu A'gen, and others, who were then sent to the Second Special Court and prosecuted on charges of obstructing official duties and inciting injury. The factory also suffered damages and hired a lawyer to file an ancillary civil lawsuit. The details of the trial have been reported in previous newspapers. The case has now been concluded. Yesterday, Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the first criminal court and sentenced Wang Diansheng to three months of imprisonment for obstructing public officials from performing their duties. Zhao Muhai, Ren Youfeng, and Xu A'gen were each sentenced to six months of imprisonment for openly gathering a crowd to use violence and coercion against public officials performing their duties. The number of days of detention before the judgment was finalized was counted as two days to offset one day of imprisonment. The other parts of the lawsuit were acquitted. The ancillary civil lawsuit was transferred to the civil court of this court for trial.
