Women's World

Not Optimistic 298

— Bi Yao

After respectfully reading Dr. Hu Shih's article "Optimism in the Pessimistic Voices" published in the Dagongbao this month on the thirteenth, I don't know how many times I hesitated over the following paragraph.

"But the greatest and most easily overlooked progress in these twenty-three years is the social reforms in various aspects. The most obvious, of course, is the liberation of women. In terms of physical health, Chinese women around the age of twenty now not only have restored their health, but are also gradually becoming the most beautiful women in the world... In addition, the increase in women's economic and legal status, the increase in the number of women participating in professional and social political careers, the gradual changes in marriage customs, and the improvement of the social status of divorced women and remarried women are all major progress in Chinese society in the past twenty years."

Women have made such great progress in the past twenty years, and it is considered the greatest progress in China. We women can smile now! I am willing to sing in unison Mr. Shao Yuanchong's National Day song: "Drum it, citizens! Sing it, citizens! ... Internal peace and external defense, the country is prosperous and the people are healthy! The martial heroes shake the eight wildernesses! How dare those ugly things violate the natural order!" to express the joy in my heart!

However, on the other hand, throughout the country, public prostitutes, private prostitutes, dance hall prostitutes, wild pheasants running rampant, modern degeneration... all women selling their flesh, although there are no accurate statistics, I estimate that in the past twenty-three years, there have been at least more than twenty-three times more of them, right? Unable to stand on their feet in the countryside, they poured into the cities, exposing themselves to the public; finding a place to eat in the cities, they endured the humiliation and abuse of employers or foremen; unable to find a place to eat, they lay "shamelessly" in the crowded streets; these are things that women twenty-three years ago did not have. Even leaving aside the lower classes of society, how can the upper and middle classes of society not be sad? This year, what everyone is talking about about women is that they still can't find a proper way out, can't find a noble career, so they take women as the weak to relieve boredom and vent their anger? Isn't it that the thought of treating women as something to be bullied, ridiculed, and played with that existed twenty-three years ago has not been torn apart at all?

Furthermore, in terms of women themselves, how much correction and reform have they been given from their families, schools, and society regarding the old tunes of dependence, obedience, vanity, conservatism, and other evils? The two or three outstanding and fortunate women have indeed gained a good position in society, but as far as women as a whole are concerned, this can only be regarded as climbing high and dangerously like a trumpet vine. If we are increasingly satisfied with this phenomenon and ignore the fact that the masses of women are in dire straits, it will only show that our women's movement is a bean sprout with insufficient sunlight and water; the higher it stretches, the weaker and more prone to withering it becomes! How can this be optimistic? If it is like Liu Chan, the Latter Ruler of Shu, who was detained in Luoyang and still claimed "I am so happy here that I do not miss Shu," then what is there not to be optimistic about?

The thoughts, habits, and various lifestyles of society still trample women underfoot. We don't care that there were Mencius's mother and Tai Si three or four thousand years ago, and we don't particularly care that there was Empress Wu and Ban Zhao three or four thousand years ago; we only hope that there is true gender equality and liberation now.

Many foreigners praise us a few times when they come to China; some time ago, a foreign writer even said he wanted to marry a Chinese woman, but soon he still embraced an American woman. Therefore, all insincere compliments, even if the speaker is well-intentioned, are nothing more than the kindness of an elder brother to ease the mind of a dwarf. We are really not optimistic about Dr. Hu's optimism.

The Work of Modern Soviet Women (Continued) 299

— By M. E. Walker, Translated by Xue Jihui

Regarding medicine, I also observed another situation: women can do medical research work. I found that the director of a large microbiology institute was a middle-aged, short-haired woman surrounded by microscopes, artificially cultivated microbes, antitoxins, etc. While she was talking to me, one eye was still watching a test glass tube full of broth, speaking about her and her assistants' recent work, which was the movement to eradicate malaria in southeastern Russia. It was very interesting that her male colleagues obeyed her orders like ordinary students, without any resistance.

In a relatively large city, I saw that all the educational experiments in progress were full of female staff. All the staff in libraries and museums are usually women; men are rare in such buildings. They are well-educated, and their positions are conditional on being able to give lectures on art, literature, or music. In the work of this group, I also found that some women organized educational tours, giving interesting lectures on history or antiquities in the neighboring cities where they lived.

The nursery system allows female workers in factories or women working in the fields to hand over their children to a group of trained caregivers while they are at work. The government has no regulations regarding this system; in fact, the organization of all such nurseries is managed entirely by women. This may be because Russians cannot suppress their individuality and remove human relationships in their simplest actions. Another type of woman specializes in managing kindergartens. In the south, I saw a very beautiful city by the sea. The methods they use to teach children seem to be a combination of several systems of Froebel, Montessori, and N.E.U., yet unlike any of them. The children are of course very happy, full of meaning, often expressed in sand piles, perforated paper, or loess. Outsiders may be surprised at how Russia deals with speculators and criminals—their punishments are usually very severe—but there is actually no secret. A large team of women specializes in this work. They mingle with the shoppers in the vegetable market or on the busy streets of the city while buying things. They pay close attention to everyone passing by. They are very familiar with all the tricks of fraud, especially those that harm the interests of the state. Therefore, these behaviors rarely escape their keen observation. They are clearly the great enemies of deceivers; if they discover fraudulent behavior, there will be severe punishment. If the deceived person is a worker, they will be dealt with even more severely. If the person who takes advantage is not a righteous worker, their punishment will be even more severe.

In fact, education in Soviet Russia is entirely managed by women. Almost all important positions in the Ministry of Education are occupied by women. They have the power to appoint new teachers and to review textbooks. They are engaged in promoting adult education and eliminating illiteracy. They pay particular attention to the education of new recruits, so the countryside is full of educational slogans and posters. Traveling cinemas often travel from one city to the next with films and pictures to promote the prevention and treatment of various epidemics. Women are often part of the staff in vehicles carrying such propaganda materials.

Moscow has a special agency that specializes in studying all aspects of female labor in factories. Each industrial building has its branch office, which manages all female labor in Russia. No female worker can be dismissed without the approval of this agency; even if a female worker is suspended for inappropriate conduct or other errors, she must wait until a second position has been found for her before she can voluntarily transfer and be managed by a new superior. Women not only manage all matters concerning women in commerce and industry, but also participate in the management and supervision of the following matters: the receipt and expenditure of funds, the surplus of profits, the insurance of all employees and goods, the taxes payable by employers, the standard inspection of goods when they leave the factory, the amount of work required by each worker, the convenience afforded to trainees during their work, the clubs established in various industrial centers, organized entertainment time, and various facilities for illiterate workers to learn to read and write.

Women have already achieved very outstanding results and at the same time are not constrained by unreasonable jealousy in the legal profession. I spent an entire afternoon in the office of a motherly female lawyer, listening carefully to appeals of various grievances that might be settled without going to court. I was very happy to listen there. Most of the litigants are farmers, who are mostly in disputes with their neighbors over various farming tools, household items, and livestock. An old man came to ask if there was any way to get the new young doctor to re-install the teeth he had extracted the week before; he was completely against this new treatment method because his old friends no longer revealed his lips. An angry young woman came to protest the spitting habits of the elderly people she lived with, which violated the ban. After office hours were over in the afternoon, the good lawyer gave me the case records to look at, which were to be sent to a female clerk in the local court. The female clerk's responsibility is to check whether the summonses are correct and whether the witnesses appear on time. This is another position that women have only recently participated in. If we unfortunately have to go to court, I believe that the annoying situation of not keeping time will be reduced by at least 50 percent.

One day, the light in the room where I lived was broken, so I notified the female inspector of the public lighting administration. I was wrong; I notified the female supervisor of the public utility bureau. This public utility bureau manages water, electricity, transportation, and street cleaning. I thought that the repair work was also under its jurisdiction. The female inspectors here pay close attention to the conditions of all public bathhouses, public laundries, and cooperative residences. Damaging or wasting public property is punished very severely. They fixed the broken light in a very short time. If they are just as quick with other tasks, then there must be very few residents in this city who feel dissatisfied with all the facilities.

What is felt after contacting modern Soviet women is that the overall trend in this country is to bring women out of the home and entrust them with the management of the country's needs for honest and compassionate work. There is no doubt that Soviet women can be faithful and responsible for their work. She has completely overturned a system that the world has long accepted, that is, the system that regards men as the sole driving force of local and central government. Even the harshest critics cannot deny that their judgment has no obvious errors, nor do they shrink from difficulties.

All the women's work I have seen shows a missionary-like spirit. This spirit is probably inspired by the fearless spirit of the women who encouraged adventurous migration in primitive times. It seems to be the great source of transforming the entire life of the Soviet Russian nation. As for emotion, it has absolutely no place. What binds it together is a continuous chain composed of cooperative links. Each link is forged from enthusiasm, and the number of new links being forged is limitless. This is work, work with will and purpose—a new system. (End)

The last paragraph of the previous issue was misprinted by the typesetter. It is reprinted and corrected in this issue. Please pay attention to the readers and apologize to the translator. Editorial Office

A Brief Description of Contraception 300

— Doctor Guo Taihua

Contraception and abortion, although their motives and purposes are often the same, differ entirely in nature and severity in legal and social issues. After all, no matter how rigidly those who adhere to the old morality may be, they can never recognize the killing of immature sperm as a violation of criminal law. And in the real world of economic collapse and complex human affairs, who does not know the importance of the theory of birth control? Therefore, I will briefly describe the methods of contraception as follows.

(A) Natural Contraception

(1) Periodic Contraception: Women ovulate every month, mostly during the eight days from the 12th to the 19th day before menstruation. An egg is released on one day. This is a fact recognized by physiologists and gynecologists in recent years. Therefore, last year, Dr. Ogino of Japan wanted to formulate a periodic contraception method based on this ovulation period, that is, to prohibit sexual intercourse within these eight days. In the monthly menstrual cycle, all days other than these eight days are called infertile periods, and sexual intercourse can be carried out at will, and natural infertility can be achieved. This method is actually of little effect, because the ovulation period of women is indeed only within these eight days, but after sexual intercourse, the survival period of sperm in the female reproductive organs is not as short as Dr. Ogino predicted. Because if sperm reaches the uterine cavity and the lower end of the fallopian tube, it can survive for 21 to 24 days. That is, at the time of sexual intercourse, although the egg has not been released, the sperm can wait in the reproductive organs. When the egg is released into the fallopian tube several days later, the sperm can still combine with the egg for pregnancy even 21 days after sexual intercourse. Therefore, the application of this method often fails. As far as the author knows, there are countless women who conceive two or three days before menstruation and one to four days after menstruation. These two or three days before menstruation and one to four days after menstruation are of course the so-called safe period by Dr. Ogino. It can be seen that this periodic contraception method is not reliable.

(2) Coitus Interruptus: That is, suddenly stopping sexual intercourse before the male is about to ejaculate. This method is difficult to implement and has a very bad impact on both husband and wife. It should not be used.

(3) Reduced Sexual Intercourse: That is, reducing the number of sexual intercourses. This method not only cannot prevent pregnancy, but also makes it easier to conceive.

(4) Specific Ejaculation Method: When the male ejaculates, he ejaculates outside the vulva, or presses the lower part of the prostate gland with his hand to make the semen turn back halfway. This method is also difficult to implement, and both the physical and mental health of both parties are adversely affected. Especially the method of pressing back halfway can cause swelling, inflammation and pain in the male urethral corpus spongiosum, which is even more harmful.

(B) Artificial Contraception

(1) Mechanical Contraception: For men, there are caecum penile sheaths, rubber penile sheaths, and glans sheaths. This method is more effective for contraception, but the sheath often has slight cracks, and sperm will flow out from the broken hole, so it still cannot prevent pregnancy, and it is very harmful to both husband and wife, especially to the woman. Frequent use can lead to female frigidity, hysteria, chlorosis, anemia, and other diseases; for men, it can lead to mental depression, premature ejaculation, and general weakness, which is no different from the harm of frequent masturbation. Therefore, this method should not be used frequently; female contraceptive devices include cervical caps, uterine suppositories, vaginal balls, uterine needles, and sponge plugs, etc.; except for the cervical cap, the other four are not very effective and are very harmful, such as cervical ulceration, uterine inflammation, and cervicitis, etc. Only the cervical cap is relatively usable, but the cervical cap must be purchased according to the size of the woman's cervix. At the same time, it is difficult to put on the cervical cap by oneself, even if someone else puts it on, it is often not put on the cervix correctly, so sperm can still enter the uterus from tiny gaps and conceive, so the effect is often inaccurate, and the cervical cap can also cause cervicitis and cervical erosion.

(2) Washing Contraception: That is, after sexual intercourse, use a gynecological douche with acidic medicinal liquid or weak sterilizing medicine to wash the vagina, such as salicylic acid, carbolic acid, boric acid, Lysol, etc. with 2% warm boiled water 98%. Although this method is effective, it is very harmful. Because this type of medicinal liquid that can kill sperm always has a stimulating effect. Over time, the nerves of the vaginal mucosa become numb, or vaginitis or cervicitis and other harms occur, and the application is also more cumbersome.

(3) Pharmaceutical Contraception: This refers to the contraceptive medicines made in various countries and sold in pharmacies. Because this type of over-the-counter contraceptive medicine is easy to use, it is only inserted into the bottom of the vagina before sexual intercourse, so most ordinary contraceptive women use it. However, there are countless products of this type of contraceptive medicine in various countries, with many names and different types. Now I will briefly describe several of its main components, such as potassium permanganate, boric acid, alum, tannic acid tartrate, cinchona bark, etc. They are all intended to kill sperm. However, due to the limited medicinal power, the sperm cannot be killed completely. Sometimes it is often ineffective.

(4) X-ray Contraception: Using appropriate X-ray irradiation can also prevent eggs from maturing and being released during a specified period of three, four, six or seven years. However, even if an experienced X-ray expert is irradiating, a slight negligence can often lead to permanent infertility, and endocrine abnormalities can occur, causing adverse effects on the whole body.

(5) Serum Contraception: Invented by Touessinov and Katcha of Soviet Russia. The fundamental theory is Spermiimmunitaet. Recently, biologists from Germany and the United States have also begun to study it. This method is to first inject live sperm into the blood of a certain animal. The blood in this animal's body will naturally produce a kind of antagonistic immune element to fight and destroy sperm. Then take this serum with antagonistic sperm immune element and make it into a contraceptive injection needle. It is said that Soviet Russia has recently produced this type of serum contraceptive needle. The theory of this method is also very correct. Animal experiments have been successful in Soviet Russia. However, what is the effect of implementing it in humans? Does it have any adverse effects on the human body? Because the author of this article has not used it, and experts from various countries have not yet made detailed announcements, so it is not known. At the same time, this type of injection seems to be not yet sold in our country.

(6) Endocrine Fluid Contraception: Women no longer continue to ovulate and have no menstruation during pregnancy. This is the inhibitory effect of the corpus luteum and placental endocrine. Therefore, recently, doctors in various European and American countries, based on this theory, have used corpus luteum and placental endocrine agents for injection as short-term contraception, that is, ovulation stops for one to two months after one injection, and pregnancy cannot occur. When the time comes, another injection is given on schedule. Recently, the Jnfeundin contraceptive drug produced in Germany and other so-called needle drugs are mostly made according to this theory. The theory of this method is indeed correct, but the existing preparations have not been researched for a long time, so they have not been refined and purified. In terms of application, the expected effect is often not achieved. In the near future, European and American countries may invent more ideal and complete preparations based on this theory and many experiments.

(7) Surgical Contraception: Using surgery to remove the testicles of men or the ovaries of women by a doctor can of course permanently prevent pregnancy. However, the mental and physical health of both men and women will be greatly affected, so it can never be used. The removal of the vas deferens, fallopian tubes, and uterus also causes permanent infertility. If fertility is needed again, it is impossible to save it. Other methods of ligating the vas deferens and fallopian tubes also have the disadvantage of permanent infertility. Therefore, among surgical contraception methods, the fallopian tube displacement method is relatively good. If you want to have children again, you can have another surgery to move the fallopian tubes back to their original position, and you can still conceive as usual. However, using surgery for contraception seems to be making a big deal out of a small issue.

In summary, under the modern medical situation, many contraceptive methods, except for surgical methods, cannot be called absolutely safe, but they only reduce the chance of conception relatively. And the endocrine fluid method and the serum method. If they can be researched and completed in the future. Or they are close to ideal and promising.

According to a recent survey by the Health Bureau of the Japanese Ministry of Internal Affairs, the average marriage ages of men and women in various countries in the world are shown in the following table. Unfortunately, China, which is known for its early marriage, is not included.

Years Years Years

Women of Jilin 302

— Li Kui

At first glance, these five characters "Women of Jilin" seem to have nothing to say. As if the women of Jilin are no different from the women of other places: in the cities, there are many wives and young ladies kept by the rich, and many prostitutes and secret prostitutes who specialize in satisfying men's desires; in the countryside, there are many virtuous wives and good mothers who specialize in raising children, cooking, and making clothes for their husbands... These are almost the same in all provinces. Of course, I can't say anything new.

In this way, I have nothing to say? Not at all! The women I want to talk about are definitely not these women who are no different from those in other provinces; but a kind of women who have special characteristics. They look the same as the women in other places; but the lives they live and the things they do are different from the women in other places.

There were not many of these women before the "September 18th" Incident; only in the countryside of Yanji and Wangqing counties; after the "September 18th" Incident, the number of these women increased. Not only did the number of these women increase in these two counties; but also in Panshi and Huadian counties, there were also these women.

They are the same as men; they want to wear the clothes of the righteous army. Needless to say, you can't tell they are women at a glance; even if you look closely, you feel that they are the same as men.

The men in the volunteer army in these four counties (of course, in addition to these four counties, there are others; but these four counties are the most) do not distinguish between nationalities; there are Koreans and Chinese; of course, women are also the same as men, and they do not distinguish between nationalities.

After the "September 18th" Incident, the power of the volunteer army in these four counties expanded even more, and they organized many vanguard teams, daredevil teams... Each team has one-third of women working. Some of them go to the front line to fight against the Japanese and "Manchukuo puppet state" troops; some do work in the rear.

Their marriages are not bound by the old ethics, nor are they controlled by money; their marriages are absolutely free. For example, when they and their lovers fall in love to the point of marriage, they immediately move in together to cohabitate.

Although their lives are very hard (because they feel a lack of material things due to the oppression of the Japanese), their spirits are indeed happy; when they do things, they are always very agile, practical, and energetic; so the men call them "happy people!"

The Starting Point of Women's Relief Work 303

— Bi Yi

The lives of Chinese women are of course very painful, but the only way to implement relief is to rely on women's own efforts. Begging for pity from others will ultimately be of no avail; but in the current situation, how can these oppressed women who have lost their ability to help themselves alleviate their suffering? It is necessary to seek it from the existing relief work in society. Regarding relief work, in theory and implementation, countries may have slight differences due to different backgrounds and positions; but it originates from the human nature of sympathy and mutual assistance, which is the same in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. However, if this point of sympathy and mutual assistance is taken as the basis for relief work, the result will be that society will only add a group of idlers. At its extreme, it can make the entire nation sink! Especially in today's China, when the nation is weak and the country is in danger, we have to talk about the issue of women's relief. It is necessary to recognize the following two points:

(1) Relief is for no relief; in other words, relief is for the sake of avoiding relief. American sociologist Edward T. Devine said in his book Principles of Relief; "The beauty of wisdom teaches people to help themselves. And through material and spiritual assistance, develop the independence and frugality of the relieved." Therefore, the fundamental purpose of relief should be to educate and increase the knowledge of the relieved on how to live a useful life, and not to cultivate dependence. This is the principle that all relief work should follow, and it is not unique to women's relief.

(2) The decline in the status of Chinese women and the suffering in their lives, although somewhat disjointed and irrelevant; but point out the defects of the social, economic, educational system, so that women lose their ability to help themselves and have to ask for help. Therefore, those unfortunate women who are kept in relief institutions should not only be educated to develop their ability to make a living, but also to improve their status, break all ideas and systems that value men over women, and cultivate their independent personality. This is a point that must be clearly recognized when discussing women's relief.

We use these two points to measure the so-called women's relief institutions in Shanghai today; some raise without teaching, some don't even talk about teaching, and even raising can't be satisfied; some take care of teaching, but the results are not good. All the houses are either crude or borrowed, and the poor equipment cannot be denied. Some institutions, although they have definite funds, have no measures, which is really a pity. As for those who run this business, most of them are stupid, old-fashioned, and lack of knowledge, which is a common phenomenon everywhere. Therefore, although the name and regulations of the Qingjie Hall are still in place, there should be no perfect place for educating and raising prostitutes and other oppressed women.

The management of women's relief institutions in Shanghai is so corrupt. Naturally, it is hoped that the government will determine the direction and reform them based on the above theories. It is also hoped that women's movement groups will do this practical work to supplement the government's shortcomings. In the current situation where both public and private economies are tight, there is no need to talk empty talk about how idealized the formal equipment should be; but there are not a few charitable institutions in Shanghai with considerable assets, but they will not make good use of them, so there is no hope for the development of the business. After that, the part of the business related to women's relief should be concentrated and unified in one place to avoid the current problems of being divided and scattered and acting on their own; the form should only be clean and need not be beautiful; in terms of spirit, it cannot be separated from the two points mentioned above. This is the starting point of women's relief work, and a slight difference will lead to a great deviation.

Supplement to Shenbao Local Edition, Amateur Weekly

Amateur Chat

The Meaning of Life, Where Does It Lie? 304

— Shao Wen

Because each person's life is different, and their views vary, there are various different explanations for the meaning of life. A miser says that the meaning of life lies in making money; people should live and die for money. A poet who worships the goddess Venus says that the meaning of life lies in love; people live for love and their reproductive organs. Pessimists say "life is like a dream," and that everything is meaningless... These are all explanations of the meaning of life from people's own standpoints.

However, we cannot therefore say that life has no definite meaning at all, and that there are only various views or philosophies of life held by different people. We cannot say that, because while there are many different opinions on this issue, and these opinions all have a certain social basis, we cannot consider them all to be correct, and therefore place them all on the same line, saying that the meaning of life can be interpreted in many ways and cannot be definitively judged. We know that truth has its relativity and its absoluteness. The interpretation of the question "Where does the meaning of life lie?" also has its relative and absolute meaning. In the relative relationship of various different interpretations, each interpretation is correct. But in a certain time and space, there is a correct interpretation among these relative interpretations, and this correct interpretation is absolute. Therefore, no matter how many opinions there are on the question of life, we can still find the meaning of life.

Human knowledge has developed to the point where we recognize the following things:

First of all, humans are the most intelligent of all things. Humans not only have feet and hands, but also a special brain; they not only have instincts, but can also act consciously. Other animals can only instinctively rely on their claws or other things to survive; they can only adapt to the environment, not change it. Humans are different. They can make tools and use tools to conquer nature. They not only adapt to the environment, but can consciously change it. Therefore, humans can improve their lives day by day, can progress from eating raw meat and drinking blood to eating fine cuisine and drinking beer, and can progress from living in caves to living in dozens of stories high buildings, and even to higher stages. Humans are animals that evolve day by day, not animals that degenerate.

At the same time, humans are social animals and cannot exist without society. The so-called evolution of mankind is the evolution of society. Obviously, in primitive society, humans could only eat raw meat and drink blood, and live in caves. Only after a contemporary society exists can they eat fine cuisine and live in tall buildings. The ability of humans to progress from eating raw meat and drinking blood and living in caves to living in buildings and eating fine cuisine is acquired with the social evolution from primitive society to modern society. Therefore, if humans want to improve their lives day by day, and make their lives more comfortable and beautiful, they must work hard to promote social evolution.

However, not all people in society welcome social evolution. In fact, under certain people's realistic, special life conditions, they not only do not promote social evolution, but desperately try to prevent the wheels of history from moving forward. The opposition of feudal aristocrats to scientific civilization in the past, and the oppression of all progressive movements of mankind by modern imperialism, are all manifestations of attempts to hold back the advancing wheels of history and to implement regression. Therefore, to promote social evolution and improve human life, we must not only fight against nature, but also fight against those who prevent social progress. The evolution of human society is the development of the contradiction of mankind's continuous struggle with nature and the continuous conflict with human beings themselves.

The so-called meaning of life lies in striving to conquer nature and fighting against all forces that prevent human progress, so as to promote the evolution of human society, so that human beings can live better. If we don't think this is the case, then where does the meaning of life lie? Is it really necessary for people to live a life of drunken dreams? Or should we really turn the wheels of history backwards and return to the Middle Ages or even the ancient times of eating raw meat and drinking blood? I think that as long as people are not degenerate to the point of being irredeemable, as long as they are not absolute advocates of degeneration, they will never give an affirmative answer to this.

Some people here are probably going to ask: In the present, how should we promote the evolution of society? Our answer is: Truth is concrete, and the solution to problems is also concrete. At present, to concretely determine how to promote social evolution, we must concretely understand the current reality. Because we must rely on the actual situation to determine the specific methods for promoting social evolution, and also to concretely determine the direction in which we should strive in life, that is, to concretely determine the meaning of our lives. Otherwise, we will become utopians. For example, people living in the Middle Ages, if they do not care about the real situation and only think about progress and leaps, trying to jump to the "kingdom of freedom" all at once, that is an illusion, a utopia. It must be known that human society evolves gradually, and it must be based on a certain realistic foundation before it is possible to evolve to a higher stage. Under this possibility, human efforts can have results, otherwise it will be in vain. The so-called meaning of life is to make concrete decisions based on the real situation under the principle that mankind should promote social evolution.

Amateur Studies

Basic Knowledge vs. Specialized Knowledge 305

— Ruo Fu

All human knowledge and learning does not come from the vast space, but is a product of society. Long before human society appeared, there would never be knowledge about science, philosophy, politics, economics, art, literature... in the universe, and therefore there would be no academic existence. The idealist Schopenhauer said in his "The World as Will and Representation": "...Even if the universe did not exist, if there was the existence of wind, there would still be music." What a mysterious statement! Think about it, without a certain rhythm and harmony, just blowing wind, how can it be called music? It must be known that music is also artificial, and it is also produced from the labor life of human beings. Without people, without human society, there would never be the existence of music.

Because all academics are products of society, we must understand them from a social point of view, no matter whether we are studying politics, economics, philosophy, science, art, literature... or even technical knowledge. No matter what subject you specialize in, you must have a basic knowledge of social science in order to enter the field and explore its essence and its occurrence and development. Otherwise, you will enter a mysterious realm and be unable to extricate yourself.

At the same time, studying any subject requires correct methods, otherwise there will be no way to start. In this regard, philosophical knowledge is even more indispensable for researchers of all subjects. Because from a methodological point of view, philosophy is the foundation of social sciences, natural sciences... Without philosophical thinking, without scientific methods, any subject cannot be recognized or grasped. Therefore, any expert must not only have general social science knowledge, but also have the basic theory of philosophy, otherwise, their research is still problematic.

There are many natural scientists, artists, writers... in society who do not understand the importance of general social science knowledge and basic philosophical knowledge. They only know how to bury themselves in their specialized subjects, despise social sciences and philosophy, and sing the song of "science for science" and "art for art"... As a result, other than kneeling before God and begging for solutions to problems, they are dominated by money bags and become slaves to money. In modern times, there are many natural scientists, such as the famous Newton, Thomson.

Page 22

Eddington... In the end, did they not think that science could not explain the mysteries of the universe and desperately support God? Hasn't the so-called "art for art" theory become the entity of "art for money"? These are all obvious examples.

However, conversely, the ability of a subject to exist independently must have its own characteristics, its own content and form. Therefore, no matter what subject the researcher is, in addition to having general social science knowledge and basic philosophical knowledge, they should also strive to study the subject they are studying and specialize in it. Because human knowledge has developed to the present, every academic department has complex materials that must be studied, and has rich content. If you do not specialize in research, the result will not be to deepen your research. We can say that no matter how great a social scientist or philosopher is, if he does not have a considerable long-term study of natural science or literature and art, and does not have specialized knowledge of natural science or literature and art, then he cannot talk about natural science or literature and art. Even if he wants to talk about it, the result will only be a big joke, and he will not get anything!

Art World

Stage Design 306

— Wei Fan

In order to enhance the divinity of the drama, the stage design must first be considered; because the size, depth, and angle of the stage, as well as its suitability for a change in the plot and its power to emphasize it, are the basic conditions for the success of a drama.

Since the stage has such an interconnected relationship with the drama, we cannot arbitrarily ignore the skills of stage design. Now let's first talk about the effect of stage design on helping actors, and how it has an inseparable connection with the audience's line of sight.

Stage design is based half on the construction of architecture and half on the axes built on the drama itself.

In the theater or in real life, no matter when, once a scene has an object, there is such an effort; to keep the eyes on a line that is perpendicular to the line of action. In a dialogue between two or more people, or when something moves from one side to the other, or in a revolving scene, such as a military parade or a competition, the most convenient thing for observation is to provide the audience with a line of sight that is at right angles to the line of action. The theater for the audience in this imagined state is arranged axially. The more fully the action can conform to this requirement, that is, to obtain the position that is perpendicular to the line of sight of the imagined audience, the more balanced the center of gravity of the action between the collaborators (two) becomes. If the axis of the performance forms any other angle, or is parallel to it, the dramatic effect of the element facing the audience will increase, otherwise it will decrease: if the actor enters from the rear or the rear steps, his effect will be greater than that of his companion who is facing away from the audience.

Speaking of stage design, it has undergone many changes in history. In ancient China, a drama group did not pay attention to the stage department: even in modern times, stage design was still influenced by Europe.

The original European stage only used the law of that single vertical axis.

In later Greek theaters, in addition to the entrance and exit in the middle, there were also entrances and exits on the left and right sides of the rear; the design technique was like the stage of Chinese Peking Opera now. On the oldest Spanish stages, there seemed to be something different, with only side entrances and exits, as if in the style of the ancient "comedy school." When the number of left and right entrances and exits increases, and at the same time the central axis increases, this law is very effective. This is the law of a single stage coordinate, which originated in Italy in the 16th century, and later gradually became popular throughout Europe, and the United Kingdom also imitated it at the same time; the current stage design of Chinese Peking Opera is probably derived from this Italian law?

The earliest decorative expression of the axis of the drama is the door; the door designated for actors to enter and exit was a decorative symbol in the Middle Ages. Later, it gradually became more beautiful, and then there was the setting of scenery; the scenic theater had some doors along the central axis of the theater or perpendicular to it, leading the audience's line of sight to those doors, the area of ​​the stage performance. Therefore, in principle, there is no difference between the medieval theater and the "humanist" theater for those axes.

Those actual entrances and exits along the line of the side curtains obviously correspond to some entrances and exits that were built from the left and right of the house in the scenic theater; the construction of the theater here is just an enclosed space, which is consistent with the principle of the drama.

Anyway, this is a fact; the depth of the stage has gradually shrunk since the eighteenth century, allowing for a second life mark, a wide coordinate of action; this improvement not only helped the successful effect of the drama, but also saved a lot of space.

In our law of dealing with stage design according to a certain axis of the drama, the deep stage only provides some side entrances and exits, and its position is at right angles to the central axis of the building. In this way, the side curtain is regarded as a particularly important element in the design.

Stage design is a clever organization of a given space, built on a virtual given axis, that is, the line of sight of the imagined audience; if the development of that technology fully allows the space to be used in all aspects, and all of the space is completely used to serve the drama, then the material of the stage design 丨 the stage itself 丨 will be more harmonious with the drama.

The current Chinese stage does not seem to have any improvements; even if there are some improvements, it is only that the technique of changing scenery is more agile. This refers to the skills of Peking Opera stage design. As for spoken dramas, it is difficult to judge because of the different environmental relations; because China currently does not have a fixed stage for performing spoken dramas, the design is only a temporary arrangement suitable for the drama to be performed, and it is not possible to talk about a truly complete design for a while!

Overseas Communication Network

Broadway Street Women 308

— Luo Lun

Portland, USA Correspondence

Americans all have the addiction of three W's: wine and women are especially important. Because of this, and in that environment, the United States has produced many prostitutes.丨丨 Although I am not an old moralist, I seem to believe what a Chinese worker said:

"Except for women who have not yet developed, there is almost no virgin in the United States!"

The women of rich families are too romantic, and the environment makes them know how to fall in love as soon as they develop. Yes, the first love of women who have just developed is willing to dedicate their hymen to men: the women of poor families, either are raped, or are willing to prostitute themselves for the sake of life, or they work during the day, and at night they are "street women." Every port's Broadway Road is full of wine and women, and this place is the same.

Today is Sunday, and I got a rest, so I followed my companion into a low-class theater, 丨丨 I still use Chicago's words to criticize it, but in fact this place can be said to be middle-class. The film being shown seems to be something like Garbo's —— these female stars seem to be out of date. I came here just to rest and relieve the boring life. There, you will find a dilapidated arrangement, the chairs are old, the walls are leaning, but it is full of people, many women are mixed in the middle of men.

I saw several Chinese workers I knew, they were all carrying low-class "street women" such as black women to watch the show.

In our front row there were some women who had not yet found men. When the lights were still on, they all looked at us, and I was afraid of them, because these women would arbitrarily talk to you to seduce you. I was going to change seats, but the whole theater was full.

The lights went out, and in my imagination, an older American woman, who was about thirty years old, turned her head and teased me:

"Aren't you too lonely?"

"No!"

I felt her hand move to my back. At the same time, I also found another woman telling jokes to my companion, 丨丨 he is older than me, so he is happy to talk to them. After a long time, the woman turned around again:

"Can I sit next to you?"

"That doesn't matter, but there are no seats?"

It was full of people. She said this too unsmartly, so she didn't say it again. 丨丨 I saw her ugly face covered with powder and rouge looking around in the dim light.

"You're coming to my house tonight!"

Suddenly I heard my companion's "opponent" begging him like this. I was really afraid that he would lose his footing, so I twisted his thigh with my hand. In this uneasy disturbance, we finally managed to spend two hours, and we all got up to leave. Who knew that those American women were all following us closely, and even approached us, just like a couple. They all asked for our hands to be held with their attitude, but this was impossible. She took my hand, put it close to my face, and said sweetly:

"Come to my house and sit for a while, Chinese!"

"No, I have to go to work!"

All the way to the door, I took off her hand, and so did my companion, and we got rid of these disturbances. We came to the center of Broadway Road, and couldn't help laughing at the same time. I haven't encountered these things in Chicago, those women only seduce you with their eyes, and they leave if they can't seduce you; I also encountered it once in de Cai, at that time in a bar, 丨丨 this is not surprising.

The lights of Broadway are gradually dimming. There are no cars after twelve o'clock. The past prosperity, only God knows its mystery; today's decline, but it is a human affair!

Shanghai Shen Bao Circulation Library Recruitment Notice for Trainees 309

Our library now intends to recruit several trainees. Those who are interested in applying for the exam, please write a letter of self-recommendation, stating the place of origin, age, family situation, mailing address, whether you are engaged or married, past schooling or employment experience, and interests, etc., and send it to "Shen Bao Circulation Library, No. 345, 3rd Floor, Continental Commercial Plaza, Nanjing Road, Shanghai" before October 25. Please indicate "Application" on the envelope, and attach a recent 4.5-inch half-length photo and return postage. Those who are suitable will be contacted for an interview, and those who are not suitable will have their photos returned. No separate reply will be given. (A) Qualifications: (1) Good health, (2) Age from 18 to 24 years old (male only for the time being), (3) Fluent in Chinese, with a junior high school graduation or equivalent level (no diploma required), (4) Honest character, quick mind, able to endure hardship and be motivated. (B) Training period: Two years. Those who have excellent results after the training period will be given priority by the library, or will be introduced as appropriate. (C) Treatment: During the training period, in addition to providing food and accommodation, a monthly allowance of 6 to 12 yuan will be given. (D) Note: After the deadline, it will take some time to review the incoming letters, so please do not urge or inquire. (Shen Bao Circulation Library)

Outlying Postal Agency

Opening Up Wasteland 310

— Liu Sha

Anqing Correspondence

In recent years, natural disasters and man-made disasters have ravaged the countryside, making it lifeless. The farmers, who are inherently conservative, cannot but run around for food and clothing and migrate in all directions. Our Anhui is a relatively barren province compared to the prosperous Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces; especially northern Anhui, which has been in famine for years, and the farmers are "not guaranteed in the morning and evening"; even the more fertile central and southern Anhui, the farmers have also been in deep water and fire in recent years. The great flood of 1931 washed away all their belongings, and the harvest disaster of last year almost made them busy for a whole year in vain. The great drought of this year is even more making them unable to live or die.

But people always have to live on, and there are always ways to live. Even disasters can sometimes help the poor. For example, floods can indeed fill millions of acres of fertile land, but they can also create a lot of arable wasteland. The "opening up wasteland" can also support a part of the common people. This kind of "opening up wasteland" has been popular in various counties near Anqing in recent years.

The causes of wasteland are roughly like this: Mountain farmers in the upper reaches, in order to avoid freezing and starvation, must try every means to harvest a little more grain to survive; so the wilderness and remote places such as the mountainside, hills, mountainside, and foothills, which were originally covered with firewood and weeds, are also planted with miscellaneous grains such as corn, sorghum, mountain potatoes, mung beans, peanuts, and sesame. The sand and soil in the mountains are all loosened, and when it rains heavily, the sand, mud, and slurry will rush down like waterfalls, and this torrent will also wash away huge amounts of sand and mud from the river bank with great force, and bring them all to the downstream. The result is naturally very unfortunate, filling many fertile lands of the farmers, the riverbed is silted up, and sometimes even the entire swamp and small lakes are filled up. In recent years, a small lake in the western countryside of Anqing has been filled up. Some large lakes are also getting smaller day by day. The riverbed is also in this situation. The famous Wan River, which originates from the Ershishan Mountains, has long become silted up and unbearable in the past ten years. Even the smallest boat is difficult to travel smoothly by the end of autumn and the beginning of winter. However, a lot of "sandbars" have grown on both sides of the river. These "sandbars" are getting bigger and bigger every year, while the bottom and body of the river are getting lower and narrower. The farmers' fertile land is gone, and their eyes naturally turn to this "God-given"
